Hungry People Gather in Washington as US Congress Opens

Over a Hundred Bills Awaiting Discussion

The Philippine Independence Bill to be First on the Agenda

▲ National News Agency, Washington, 4th. The US Congress will convene at noon tomorrow to discuss the most serious issues since the European War. After prayers, the House and Senate will proceed with the opening formalities and then begin legislative business. It is reported that over a hundred bills have been prepared by members of the House and will be successively introduced after the opening session. The following bills are planned to be introduced immediately after the opening of the House tomorrow: 1) An amendment to the Volstead Act to allow the sale and manufacture of beer containing 2.75% alcohol; 2) Convening a state convention to ultimately repeal the Eighteenth Amendment to the Constitution (i.e., lifting the alcohol ban); 3) Reducing letter postage from three cents to two cents; 4) Restricting the activities of the Federal Farm Board and prohibiting the use of public funds to maintain market prices; 5) Temporarily suspending payments on rural mortgages; 6) The US Shipping Board will permanently manage coastal and inland waterway transportation; 7) Thoroughly investigating the Treasury Department's refund of income taxes. Many bills have also been prepared in the Senate. The Philippine Independence Bill will be the first item on the agenda tomorrow. Although preparations have been made for the bill to lift the alcohol ban, it is unlikely to be brought up for discussion tomorrow.

〓Hungry Petitioners Arrive in Washington〓

Threatening to Destroy Congress

Will a Bloody Tragedy Be Repeated?

Reuters, Washington, 4th. The first group of unemployed petitioners, about 1,000 people, arrived here this afternoon by car. As they arrived, a police squad of about 150 officers greeted them and led them to a temporary camp in the woods near the railway. The area had been pre-cordoned off with ropes, and the police tricked the petitioners into the enclosure, preventing them from leaving. Despite being hungry and cold, the petitioners still sang the Internationale. Their leader, a man named Panchming, gave an angry speech to the police and journalists, stating, "We will destroy Congress, we will use force to break into the halls of Congress. If they do not accept our demands, we will riot. If Hoover calls in the army, bloodshed will be inevitable." This petition group is well-organized and has some cash. In addition, a petition group of about 1,500 people has been driven out of Cumberland, Maryland, by the "citizen army." The petition group in that area, due to a lack of food and housing, had internal conflicts and attacked their leader. Therefore, the "citizen army" of the city drove out the entire petition group and placed them in a 16-acre field to sleep outdoors. There is a six-room farmhouse in the enclosure, which is now used as housing for the women and children of the petition group.

National News Agency, Washington, 4th. Hungry petitioners and disgruntled farmers arrived in Washington today to petition Congress. The farmer representatives are temporarily staying in empty warehouses and the homes of friends. The hungry petitioners first marched through the streets and in the evening, most of them were housed in the Fort Myer barracks, which was allocated by the authorities on the condition that they maintain order, otherwise they would be expelled. Their numbers are still difficult to estimate. According to the police patrolling the parade ground in front of the barracks, there are at least 2,500 people, including several women. In addition, there are those who have rented cheap inns and dormitories in the downtown area, preparing to join the march tomorrow. Police Commissioner Fang advised the leaders of the petition group to send a few representatives to meet with the speakers of both houses of Congress tomorrow to present their demands. However, no agreement has yet been reached. The farmer representatives do not intend to take demonstrative actions, but only to organize a National Farmers Relief Conference in Washington to discuss and pass resolutions to send to Congress. These are all officially elected representatives of farmers' groups from various regions, including several who joined the withholding of grain movement this summer. However, they expressed sympathy for the hungry petitioners.

National News Agency, Washington, 4th. Three groups of hungry petitioners will arrive in Washington today, one from the South, one from the North, and one from the West, all heading towards the capital. They are said to be orderly, but the authorities are concerned about unexpected incidents and have divided the police into three teams, preparing to suppress them separately to prevent disturbances on the opening day of Congress. However, some officials today advocated allowing them to enter Washington and send representatives to Congress to petition for unemployment relief, but the regulations for assembling and marching will be strictly enforced. If the hungry petitioners are determined to march past Congress, a large armed force will be dispatched to guard and suppress them. Police Commissioner Blancard has served in the police force for forty years and is confident that his police force is sufficient to deal with the situation and that the situation is not worrying. He has made extensive preparations to prevent disturbances.

〓Disturbances Also Arise Among Mexican Hungry People〓

National News Agency, Veracruz, 4th. Mexico also has a hungry petition group today, with twice as many people as in the United States. This morning, more than 5,000 hungry men and women marched to the state capital, causing disturbances and attempting to enter the governor's office. More than 60 people were arrested by the police.

〓The United States Is Willing to Make Concessions on War Debts〓

Reuters, New York, 4th. According to a Washington dispatch from a New York newspaper, the US authorities are now considering the possibility of facilitating Britain's repayment of the debt due on December 15. According to dispatches from Washington, leading bankers have advised the government to grant a grace period. President Hoover, Treasury Secretary Mills, and Secretary of State Stimson met all day today to find a way to avoid the crisis on December 15.

Reuters, Washington, 4th. The United States criticized the British and French governments' responses regarding the deferral of war debts, focusing its attack on European military expenditures. Gore, who served as a state official in President Wilson's government, issued a suggestion today that war debts should be repaid with international bonds, and these bonds should be guaranteed by the debtor countries in proportion to their military expenditures. Senator Somers, chairman of the Senate Monetary Committee, advocated using the war debt issue to increase the price of silver, saying that the United States might as well use silver to pay off the December debt, in order to solve the future market depression.

〓Even the First Metropolis Is Running Out of Money〓

New York's Finances Running Dry

Police Salaries in Jeopardy

National News Agency, New York, 4th. New York City is the richest city in the world, but under the current circumstances, the salaries of municipal government employees and police officers on the 15th of this month may not be paid due to a lack of funds. The banks believe that the city's treasury is already heavily indebted and will not grant loans unless the municipal government greatly reduces government spending. Acting Mayor McKee has already begun to reduce government spending and has submitted a bill to reduce government spending to the state legislature, but the bill has not yet been passed, and the banks are hesitating to provide loans. The authorities are deeply concerned that after the salaries are in arrears, the police will become as undisciplined as the police in Chicago after their salaries were in arrears.

〓The Philippine Islands Convene a Special Congress〓

Tax Laws Will Be Amended

National News Agency, Manila, 5th. The Governor of the Philippine Islands has ordered the convening of a special session of the legislature to correct the errors in the legislative bills passed last time, especially the tax laws, because the hasty passage last time resulted in many errors in the general tax table, such as the cotton tax being completely forgotten.

Prospects for Disarmament Negotiations Are Bleak

France Remains Firm on Its Demand for Equality with Germany

MacDonald's Efforts at Mediation Have Been Fruitless

The International Disarmament Conference Is Likely to Be Suspended Indefinitely

Even if a Draft Treaty Can Be Concluded, It Will Be Worthless

National News Agency, Geneva, 4th. The League of Nations is becoming increasingly pessimistic about the future of disarmament issues, because according to leaked secret information, the talks between the British Prime Minister and the French Premier have been fruitless, because France refuses to make any concessions on Germany's demand for equality in armaments, and the British Prime Minister's efforts have been to no avail. It is also reported that the British Prime Minister said that "Christmas is just around the corner, and all peoples in the world should forget their hatred and engage in the promotion of friendship, so the authorities in France should also quickly adopt bold and far-reaching plans." Looking at the current situation, although German Foreign Minister Neurath has gone to Geneva from Berlin, the five-nation meeting scheduled for Sunday is unlikely to have a satisfactory outcome. Based on the general observations of observers here, the future of the conference is extremely hopeless. What is noteworthy is how the League of Nations will deal with the aftermath. Will the Disarmament Conference be suspended indefinitely thereafter, or will a draft treaty be drawn up in accordance with the US proposal to first establish the minimal effects that this conference has already achieved, but even if this draft treaty can be concluded, its value is virtually nil.

National News Agency, Paris, 4th. According to Geneva news, the Disarmament Conference may be postponed indefinitely to cover up its complete failure. The political circles here have expressed strong protests against this, saying that Herriot will still insist that the Disarmament Conference should discuss France's disarmament security plan, even if Germany does not return to the meeting. Herriot will also vigorously oppose British Prime Minister MacDonald's view that the life or death of the Disarmament Conference depends on whether Germany returns to the meeting. Italy's representative is also the same as Britain. Now the only fear is that Herriot will refuse to make any concessions to Germany and insist that the issue of equality of status must be mentioned after the end of the conference and cannot be used as a condition for participating in the conference. If this is the case, it will be a fatal blow to the conference.

Davis Actively Engaged

Reuters, Geneva, 4th. Davis, the US representative participating in the Disarmament Conference and the World Economic Conference in Europe, is now very active in promoting the US proposal to suspend the Disarmament Conference. The United States proposes that all principles that all parties can agree on should be included in a document and signed before December 15. The abolition of chemical and mold warfare, the restriction of cannons and tanks, and the prohibition of large-scale bombing of undefended towns must all be included. This is a temporary convention, supplemented by a permanent supervisory committee, which should meet on the 15th of this month and complete its work before the next Easter. This temporary convention will be the first stage of disarmament and will be valid until April 1937, so that it will expire at the same time as the Washington Naval Treaty. The Supervisory Committee will discuss the second stage of disarmament and draw up an agreement that includes all US proposals. The recognition of Germany's equality in armaments also contains restrictions on the implementation of equality in armaments. The above is the US proposal. Although there is no indication in the US proposal to exchange disarmament for war debt concessions, it is noteworthy that Davis is eager to sign this requirement before December 15.

December 15 is the date on which war debts are due. The intention is to ease the attitude of US congressmen, who are very dissatisfied with Europe's huge military spending, towards war debts. French Premier Herriot is scheduled to return to Paris from Geneva on Tuesday, and it seems that the German Foreign Minister Neurath, who will arrive here on Sunday, may not be able to agree on their outstanding issues.

Franco-German Pending Issues Are Difficult to Compromise

National News Agency, Berlin, 4th. German Foreign Minister Neurath left for Geneva tonight to attend the five-nation meeting, but political circles in Berlin have very little hope for the meeting because France has not prepared to abandon its unwillingness to accept Germany's concept of equality.

Japan Presents New Plan

(Tokyo) Japanese Disarmament Representative Tsuno, on the 4th in Geneva, presented Japan's disarmament plan to the representatives of the United Kingdom, the United States, France, Italy, and other countries. Its content is as follows: 1) This conference cannot be bound by the Washington and London treaties; 2) The reduction of armaments should be based on the current strength; 3) The reduction of offensive ship types should be the main focus. This method makes Japan sacrifice more and other countries sacrifice less, so the tonnage of each battleship should be reduced to 25,000 tons, and the caliber of the guns should be reduced to 14 inches; 4) The ratio of Japan to the United States for battleships and cruisers with 8-inch guns must be more than 70%; 5) Japan supports the complete abolition of aircraft carriers or the reduction of their tonnage; 6) Japan opposes the complete abolition of submarines.

Havas, Geneva, 5th. The Japanese representative to the Disarmament Conference formally notified the signatory countries of the Washington and London Naval Treaties of the basic principles of Japan's naval disarmament proposal. There are four main points: 1) The single tonnage of battleships should be reduced from 35,000 tons to 25,000 tons; 2) Aircraft carriers should be prohibited or their tonnage reduced; 3) Cruisers should retain 8-inch guns; 4) Submarines should be retained.

Italy Adds Two New Ships

Reuters, Rome, 4th. It is firmly denied here that Mussolini ordered the construction of two 7,000-ton cruisers because he was dissatisfied with France's continued construction of the new cruiser "Dunkerque." According to official sources, the French government's continued construction of ships has indeed made the Italian government dissatisfied, but Italy's construction of two cruisers is actually part of Italy's shipbuilding plan to replace old ships, and it is not aimed at France. It is reported that both new Italian ships are equipped with 6-inch guns.

The Interlocking Relationship Between the Manchurian Question, War Debts, and Disarmament

Russian Newspaper Claims U.S. Using War Debt Issue

To Break the Diplomatic Alliance of Britain, France, and Japan

TASS, Moscow, 4th -- The "Pravda" newspaper here today published an article discussing the second war debt note sent by Britain and France to the U.S., stating that war debts are not merely an economic issue, but a political one. The U.S. is allegedly using this to exert pressure on its competitors and break the diplomatic alliance between Britain, France, and Japan. The newspaper claims the British note's assertion that "the economic prosperity from 1923 to 1929 was illusory" is quite accurate. It argues that the heavy burden of war debt repayments would strike a blow to the finances and commerce of European nations, intensifying market competition, leading to a drop in the pound's value, higher prices, wage cuts, and increased internal instability in Britain. However, in this note, the British Empire, besides acknowledging its own weakness, also undisguisedly threatened the U.S., saying that any blow to the British economy would directly affect the U.S. economy. This point indicates that Downing Street and the Quai d'Orsay had already been in contact before the British note was issued, so the reasons given in the British and French notes, though different, are only formally different in diplomacy. Furthermore, the failure to give the same reasons also avoids arousing the fear among American creditors of a "European common front." However, there is indeed no common front in Europe, as Germany and Italy are now each going their own way. The newspaper concludes by saying that the antagonism among the powers is now becoming increasingly acute, and the issues of war debts, disarmament, and the Manchurian question are all closely interlinked and cannot be resolved separately.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 5th -- The Naval Ministry announced that, according to a telegram from the Commander of the Mako Naval Base, the destroyer "Hayasuzuki," while returning to the Mako Naval Base from the Kure Naval Port, was caught in a storm and drifted in the sea about one hundred miles north of Baogui Cape, the northern tip of Taiwan, at 2:00 PM on the 5th. Judging from the government's intentions, it merely wants to use this to get through the parliamentary difficulties. As for the ideological aspect, it is also an unprecedentedly major issue. There is the issue related to the [illegible] incident of incumbent judges. On the one hand, regarding the Manchurian policy and diplomacy, the entire country has demands on the current government. In short, such a situation cannot be opened up and rescued by superficial means such as the technicalization of finance and administration; it truly requires fundamental political and economic reforms. This is the attitude held by the National League. From this perspective, it will deal a painful blow to the government whenever it has the opportunity. On the other hand, it will pay close attention to the attitudes of the Seiyukai and Minseito and seek countermeasures to adapt to the situation.

Trotsky Secretly Returns to Paris

▲ National News Agency China-Japan, Paris -- Trotsky, using the name Sedov, arrived in Dunkirk today with his wife and three secretaries aboard a Danish ship, and then traveled here by train. The police have again increased their precautions against opponents of Trotsky engaging in demonstrations. Trotsky originally intended to reside in Denmark for a long time, so he and his wife had found a house in the Danish countryside, intending to purchase it if the Danish government allowed it, but it was ultimately rejected, reportedly out of fear of offending the Soviet Russian government. Trotsky's desire to move to Denmark was ostensibly because he wanted to consult the famous library in Copenhagen for his writing, but in reality, he wanted to be in closer contact with the development of Russian affairs. It is expected that Trotsky will soon return to Istanbul (formerly Constantinople), where he previously resided.

The Manchurian Question and Representatives of the League of Nations

The Spanish representative, Madariaga, and the Czechoslovakian representative, Beneš, are the vanguards of anti-Japanese sentiment among the small countries. Madariaga, currently 46 years old, initially worked in the railway industry, then served as the chief editor of literary reviews in London. Ten years ago, he served as a member of the press department of the League of Nations Secretariat, Minister of Disarmament, and Director-General of the International Conference on the Management of Military Supplies Trade. He is brave, astute, and has made great contributions to the disarmament cause. In April 1931, he served as the first ambassador of the Spanish Republic to the United States, and is currently the ambassador to France. He is proficient in English, French, and several other languages, and his sharp tongue has been exceptionally forceful in refuting Japan during the League Council meetings. Therefore, the Japanese deeply resent him and call him the "Head of the Mouse." Beneš is a famous European diplomat and an economist. Since the founding of the Czechoslovak Republic in 1928, he has served as the Foreign Minister to this day. He is fully aware of all the events and all the large and small issues that have occurred in Europe after the Great War. He and President Masaryk are known in Europe for their intelligence and competence. Currently 48 years old, his lifelong advocacy is to devote himself to the completion of European peace mechanisms. However, he is close to France because he has to cooperate with France in order to maintain the peace organization in Central Europe. On the one hand, he also woos the United Kingdom and France to jointly maintain the political and economic interests of Europe. If the United Kingdom and France have disputes, Beneš will step in to mediate, so he is trusted by the authorities in the United Kingdom and France. Since 1923, he has led the small countries in striving for European peace. At the Council meeting on the 25th of last month, Beneš advocated entrusting the entire Manchurian issue to a special assembly, using a simple method of deliberation, and reserving the right to state his opinions at the assembly. As soon as the representatives of various countries heard his words, the United Kingdom happily agreed, and Japan's opposition to the proposal to transfer the issue to the assembly completely failed. This must be attributed to the fact that Beneš has always been trusted by various countries.

Hymans, the President of the Council and Belgian Foreign Minister, is known to all in European diplomatic circles. He is a veteran in the European diplomatic field, and drafted the articles of the League of Nations. After the European War, he attended the Paris Peace Conference, and his tactful and smooth diplomatic skills won him the sympathy of various countries. He served as the President of the first League of Nations General Assembly. Whenever there is an international conference, he is invited to attend and provide assistance. He has made great efforts in resolving major diplomatic issues such as the Ruhr Question, the Trieste Question, the Security Treaty, and the Customs Agreement. The Customs Agreement was originally created by him. He comes from a famous Belgian family, has served as a member of the Belgian Parliament, and is proficient in literature. From 1898 to 1914, he served as a professor at the Free University of Brussels, earning the honor of a doctorate in the history of parliamentary law. He has written extensively and is respected by the representatives of the League. How the Manchurian question will be resolved is closely related to him, as his every word and action is sufficient to influence the views of the representatives of the League. He uses a liberal worldview to distinguish right from wrong, and his actions are in accordance with reason and emotion. He pays attention to the attitude of the United Kingdom towards the Manchurian question, but whether the United Kingdom can uphold justice, given the failure of the Republican Party in the United States elections, the increasing demand for German military parity, and the annual payment of 1.5 million yuan to the League, among other factors, is still questionable. However, as far as the opinions of Drummond, Lytton, and Simon, the three major figures of the United Kingdom in the League, are concerned, their views are largely the same, and Lytton, as the chairman of the investigation committee, has to uphold his own national dignity and deal with the matter fairly. This time, the Manchurian question will be deliberated according to Article 15 of the Covenant, first through a resolution of the Committee of Nineteen, and then voted on by the General Assembly. However, judging from the situation of the resolution of the Provisional Assembly on March 3rd, among the small countries, such as Spain, Panama, Ireland, Norway, Poland, Czechoslovakia, and other representatives, and the committee members from Switzerland, Colombia, Hungary, Sweden, and Turkey, nine out of ten are anti-Japanese. Although the major countries dare not offend Japan, Japan has fallen into a desperate situation of isolation and helplessness. This is why the Japanese government is unusually embarrassed and threatens to withdraw. At the welcome reception, Matsuoka, the plenipotentiary, even declared, "If Japan's claims are not implemented, kill me to show Japan's determination." Such threatening words are almost identical to Uchida's statement that "I would rather turn the whole of Japan into scorched earth than give up Manchuria." I do not know if the various countries will be intimidated by this. (End)

The attitudes of the representatives of the major countries are roughly on the one hand to maintain the authority of the League, on the other hand to appease the dissatisfaction of the small countries, and at the same time to fear Japan's strength and consider its face. Because Japan is threatening to withdraw from the League, the United Kingdom, France, Germany, and other countries are making great efforts to accommodate Japan on the Manchurian question because of war debts and military parity issues. However, the small countries believe that Japan has clearly violated the Covenant and strongly advocate sanctions, and hope that Japan will withdraw so that they can maintain the League's functions in the future.

Among the major countries, France's pro-Japanese color is relatively clear. France and Japan have long had a tacit understanding. The two representatives of France in the Council, one is General Peng Gu, Chief of the Army, and the other is General Krowatt of the investigation committee. These two will largely follow Japan's intentions. When Mr. Krowatt attended the Council meeting last month, he was still protecting Japan, as he had done in Beiping. At the meeting of the investigation committee on the 24th of last month, he opposed Lytton's advance. He said that Lytton had not consulted with the investigation committee beforehand and could not speak freely in the Council. This is enough to count the attitude of France. Mr. Chak is 61 years old and served as a military attaché at the French Embassy in China. When the investigation team was preparing its report in Beiping, the members were generally dissatisfied with Japan. The content of the report was mostly unfavorable to Japan, but due to Mr. Chak's opposition, it was revised several times. As for Peng Gu, although he has unspeakable difficulties in French policy and international relations, he originally came from the Socialist Party and has always advocated fairness, and regards the League as the supreme and inviolable. In addition, various environments and circumstances make it inconvenient to openly show a pro-Japanese attitude. However, the French government has expressed dissatisfaction with the U.S. war debt issue, so France is bound to change its attitude towards the Manchurian question. It is said that French Prime Minister Herriot will personally appear at the General Assembly on the 6th. Herriot was originally the son of a poor soldier and graduated from the Higher Normal School. He is a famous practical politician in Europe. He will shift with the attitude of the United States. If the United States does not change its original position, Herriot will definitely not be confused by Japan. As for the United Kingdom, in addition to the Conservative Party, the Liberal and Labor Parties are very anti-Japanese. Their representative, Foreign Minister Simon, is a passionate and practical member of the Liberal Party. He graduated from Oxford University, is 58 years old, initially worked as a lawyer, is famous in the British legal world, and later served as the head of the Attorney General's Office and the Home Secretary. In 1929, he served as the chairman of the Indian Constitutional Investigation Committee. The so-called Simon Report shocked the entire Europe. Although he has not yet clearly expressed his anti-Japanese sentiment on the Manchurian question, he will definitely follow the Liberal Party's intentions and implement his主張. Next is Italy. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has already expressed his intentions in his speech, but Italy has little interest in the Far East, so it does not want to offend Japan. Therefore, it is currently taking a wait-and-see attitude. The representative of the Netherlands is Foreign Minister Arocho, who served as the ambassador to Japan and is regarded by the Japanese as a pro-Japanese figure. Next is Germany. Germany is preoccupied with the issue of military parity and has no time to consider the Eastern Incident. In addition, with the resignation of the Papen cabinet and the beginning of the Schleicher cabinet, it is unpredictable whether it will be able to uphold justice in its own relationship. As for League of Nations Secretary-General Drummond, who is now 57 years old, served as the secretary of Lord Balfour, the British representative, during the Versailles Peace Conference. He is quite fair in handling affairs. This time, he has spared no effort in transferring the Manchurian question to the General Assembly and in mediating private negotiations. Although he has the power to manipulate the meeting, he dares not openly protect one side due to the extremely complex international political situation. The most noteworthy thing at the moment is the United States. With the victory of the Democratic Party in the United States elections, its representative, Davis, proposed a constructive settlement plan in order to avoid a frontal conflict between Japan and the major countries concerned. According to Japanese newspapers, Davis's so-called constructive settlement plan is that, on the one hand, it formally recognizes the existence of Manchukuo, and on the other hand, it reserves China's sovereignty.

Investigation of the Palace Museum's Sale of Objects Completed

Supervisory Committee Members Gao and Zhou Have Left Beiping One After Another

The Results of the Investigation Will Be Released After Being Submitted

Beiping News: Supervisory Committee members Gao Lu and Zhou Lisheng, who came to Beiping to investigate the Palace Museum's sale of objects, have recently completed their investigation. Gao Lu left Beiping for Qingdao a few days ago, and Zhou Lisheng also took the Beining train to Tianjin at 4:25 PM yesterday (the 1st). After reviewing the files related to the [illegible] catty price increase case, he will return to Nanjing as soon as possible to report to the Control Yuan. Beiping press circles had previously been promised by Gao and Zhou that they would release the results of the Palace Museum investigation before leaving Beiping after the investigation was completed. Yesterday, many people went to the Central Hotel to visit Zhou and inquire. Mr. Zhou suddenly said that according to the Control Yuan's practice, the results of the investigation of cases cannot be released to the public before being submitted to the Yuan. He then issued a written statement and handed it to the reporters for publication. Since the reporters could not hear the results of the investigation, they inquired about the progress of the investigation from Zhou. Zhou said that he and Mr. Gao Hanqing had been in Beiping for three weeks. Because the case was complicated, they conducted internal and external investigations. The internal investigation involved reviewing various related documents, including resolutions of the Board of Directors and the Supervisory Committee, documents submitted by the Yuan to the Executive Yuan when selling objects, and approvals from the Executive Yuan, and accounts of the sale of various objects and goldware. They either extracted original files or selected excerpts to be carried to the Control Yuan. The procedures of the Yuan for selling objects have been thoroughly investigated. Regarding the number of existing antiques, because there are a vast number of antiques, it is impossible to check them one by one. They have been checked using sampling methods. However, regarding the authenticity of the existing antiques, because examining authenticity involves expertise, they could not proceed and did not start the review. The external investigation has been conducted separately with the Yuan's supervisory committee, the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Headquarters, the Beiping Municipal Government, and the Beiping District Court. However, on the side of the Garrison Headquarters, although the Palace Museum recognized Yu Xiaohou (Xuezhong) as the Yuan's supervisory committee member, Mr. Yu strongly denied it to them. They also met with various directors of the Yuan and members of the Political Committee, such as Liu Zhe and Wang Shuhan, and investigated ancient dealers and gold shops that had purchased objects from the Yuan one by one, all of which yielded considerable results. To summarize the results of this investigation, what can be reported is: (1) The Yuan's procedures for selling objects are mostly flawed; (2) Various rumors from the outside cannot be substantiated with evidence. That's all. The written statement issued by Zhou is as follows: "Our mission to Beiping has been completed. Mr. Gao went to Qingdao the day before yesterday, and I also plan to go to Tianjin in a day or two. The investigation of the Palace Museum case has yielded considerable results, but the situation is complicated and cannot be fully explained in a few words. However, what the outside world criticizes about the Yuan includes things that are real and things that are unreal. After we return to Beijing, we will truthfully report and handle the matter in accordance with the law. The details can be made public to society in about two weeks. I am sorry that I cannot provide details at this moment. Zhou Lisheng, December 1st.

Treasures in Dorgon's Tomb Stolen

Dragon Spring Sword, Jade Cane, and Other Items Stolen Clean

The Leader of the Thieves Pretends to Be Sick and Flees to Beiping, Happening to Encounter the Victim

Beiping News: The theft of the tomb of Dorgon, the Regent Prince who founded the Qing Dynasty, by the local tyrant Bao Jintai in Changping County in collusion with Wang Fukun and others, has attracted considerable attention in society. The truth, according to the investigation, is as follows: Since Dorgon's tomb was stolen, the tomb owner Qi Liande was also brought in for questioning. After interrogation by Changping County, the leader of the thieves, Bao Jintai, and others confessed without denial. However, Bao Jintai, knowing that the case was serious, falsely claimed to be ill and requested permission to seek medical treatment outside on bail. The county government did not investigate deeply and granted bail. When the deadline for summons expired, Bao Jintai was evasive in every way and failed to appear after three summonses, secretly fleeing. The county government realized it had been fooled and was extremely alarmed by the seriousness of the case. It immediately detained the guarantor and strictly demanded that Bao Jintai be brought to justice. As soon as Bao Jintai heard of the strict arrest, he knew that it would be difficult to stand on his feet unless he fled far away. Therefore, on the tenth of last month, he secretly disguised himself and his family and took a long-distance bus to Beiping. It happened that Qi Liande, due to the county government's release of the leader of the thieves and the delay in dealing with the matter, returned to Beiping to file a complaint with the Military Commission branch and the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Headquarters. To his surprise, the enemy's road was narrow. Just as he boarded the bus, he caught a glimpse of Bao Jintai accompanied by women in the carriage, obviously fleeing to avoid punishment. At that time, he was afraid of alarming the thief and did not arrest him. When the bus arrived at Xizhimen, Qi Liande reported to the police and accused him. The gang police and others sent him to the district together for interrogation and then to the Public Security Bureau for questioning. However, Qi Liande had already filed a complaint with the Garrison Headquarters, requesting that the county be ordered to present the case to the Ministry for investigation. The original presentation is as follows: "The tombs of the princes and nobles within the ancestral tomb of Liande's ancestors are located in Shangzhuang Village, Changping County, with magnificent architecture and burial treasures, many of which are historical relics, and are the hereditary formula of the Liande family. Wang Tai, the weak tomb keeper, caused the local tycoon Bao Jintai and his sons Changren and Wang Fukun, Zhou Fu, Zhou San, etc. to steal. In the early part of the twelfth month of the old calendar last year, they colluded with Wei Yongfu, Bao Changqing and others to open up three tombs of Kuixu, Chengan, and Yulin, and stole all the sacrificial objects in the mausoleum and the treasures in the coffin. At that time, Liande was far away in Tianjin. After hearing the news, he immediately returned to Beiping and went to Changping County to verify that Bao was the accused, Bao Jintai, Bao Changren, Wang Fukun, Zhou Fu, Zhou San, etc. were captured and detained by the county. Wei Yongfu, Bao Changqing, etc. were hiding. After the county summoned witnesses and confirmed the facts, the accused also confessed to the tomb robbery. The stolen burial objects were reported to the county chief Zhang Shusen at the time, and it was informed that the defendants had stolen important treasures, including a historically famous Dragon Spring Sword, a transparent jade cane, a transparent jade white [illegible], two transparent jade flower pots, a set of pure gold five offerings, and a pair of jade lions and jade horses. Zhou Fu also confessed to having a sapphire tripod, but it has not been searched for. After a long delay, the main offender Bao Jintai was suddenly released in the seventh month of the old calendar this year, and the disaster struck again. Because Bao Jintai, once released, immediately led many people to continue to excavate the tombs of Nielehan and Harachun, stealing all the burial objects and sacrifices together. These local tycoons support the situation and are unwilling to give up their fierceness. If they are not severely punished, it will not be enough to maintain the rule of law and guarantee the future. Liande and others, descendants of the Eight Banners, are all grateful for the [illegible] and share the same fate as the Republic of China. They are heartbroken and saddened by the continuous excavation of their ancestors' tombs and the exposure of their bones. They can only request the Ministry to take charge of the maintenance and protection of the tombs for the future. It is hoped that Bao Jintai and others are all local tycoons in Changping. The county handling this case is afraid of taking into account the environment and cannot handle it thoroughly. It is hoped that the Ministry will take into account the word-of-mouth and the kindness of the flag people, and that no one will forget the benefits. They should report the facts and request that the previous case be brought to the Ministry, that the stolen goods be searched completely, and that they be handled in accordance with the law. In addition to the items that should be ordered to be led, all items related to history and culture, and the costs of repairing the tombs, should also be ordered to be compensated by the defendants in order to maintain the rule of law and serve as a warning. This is to the utmost gratitude and obedience."

Anhui Province Rice Permit Tax Abolished

Wuhu Communication: The rice export permit tax established by the Anhui Provincial Government charged six jiao per dan of rice and four jiao for miscellaneous grains. A Rice Management Committee was established to oversee these matters. After its establishment, the committee appointed prominent Anhui figures such as Lu Zhongnong and Yu Youquan as directors of the rice tax bureaus in Dashengguan and other locations. However, Anhui natives, both inside and outside the province, protested against the rice tax, viewing it as harmful to merchants and farmers. Fellow villagers in Shanghai dispatched representatives to Wuhu, Anqing, Bengbu, and other places to unite with local communities and resolutely oppose it. It is now reported that the provincial authorities, recognizing the intense public sentiment and the central government's order to cease the tax, proposed a resolution at the provincial government's regular meeting on the second of this month to abolish the rice permit tax. The road construction expenses of this province will be compensated by a special fund allocated separately by the central government. Upon receiving this news, Li Yunqi, the chairman of the Wuhu Rice Management Committee, and committee member Cheng Fuchu, have independently submitted their resignations and requested the abolition of the Rice Management Committee. It is said that the total permit fees collected by various customs stations last month exceeded 400,000 yuan. (December 3rd)

Planning the Construction of Railways in Guizhou, Guangxi, and Guangdong Provinces

Each province to send one member to the road construction committee.

Wang Xunzhi appointed as Guizhou's road construction member.

Guangzhou Communication: Before the political upheaval in Guizhou and Wang Jialie's departure, Guizhou, Guangxi, and Guangdong, with their interdependent relationship, actively pursued connections. Guizhou even sent representatives to Guangdong to foster friendship. The Southwest Political Affairs Committee, aiming to develop industries in the Southwest, facilitate transportation between the provinces, and strengthen border defense, proposed the construction of railways in Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou. The plan involved the establishment of a joint Guangdong-Guangxi-Guizhou Road Construction Committee, with each province sending one member. This proposal was passed at the 41st meeting of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and distributed to the governments of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou for compliance, urging them to promptly dispatch personnel to promote its implementation. After receiving the order, the Guangdong Provincial Government wired the chairmen of the Guangxi and Guizhou provincial governments. Recently, a sudden change occurred in Guizhou, Wang Jialie has left his post, and Mao Guangxiang is in charge. The joint effort of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou is now missing Guizhou. However, Guangxi has not forgotten the three-province road construction matter and appointed Wang Xunzhi as a member of the three-province road construction committee, informing the Guangdong Provincial Government via telegram. The exchange of telegrams between Guangdong and Guangxi is attached as follows: 1. Guangdong Provincial Government's telegram to Chairman Huang of the Guangxi Provincial Government and Chairman Wang of the Guangdong Provincial Government: "We have received Instruction No. 1679 from the Southwest Political Affairs Committee of the National Government, stating that the 41st Political Affairs Committee meeting resolved to construct the Guizhou-Guangxi-Guangdong Railway, and the matter has been assigned to the governments of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou to determine the methods and establish a committee for preparation. In addition to distributing the order, we hereby instruct your provincial government to comply, properly plan, and report back." Signed by Lin Yunjie, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government. 2. Guangxi Provincial Government's reply telegram to Chairman Lin of the Guangdong Provincial Government in Guangzhou: "We have received your respected telegram and understand the matter of constructing the Guizhou-Guangxi-Guangdong Railway to be handled by the three provincial governments of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou. We have just received the order from the Southwest Political Affairs Committee of the National Government with the same content and are planning to discuss it. According to your telegram, we have appointed Wang Xunzhi as the preparatory committee member for this matter and have separately informed the member via telegram. We hereby inform you for your reference." Signed by Huang Xuchu, Chairman of the Guangxi Provincial Government. (December 1st)

Chen Cheng Leads Troops to Suppress Fang Shao on Three Routes

The 18th Army Recaptures Xuwan and Jinxi for the Second Time.

Zhou Hunyuan Cuts off Contact Between Zhu Mao and Fang Shao.

Wei Lihuang's Troops Arrive in Jiangxi Successively to Suppress Bandits.

Nanchang Communication: Communist bandits Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Lin Biao, Peng Dehuai, Luo Binghui, and Xiao Ke have connected with Fang Shao in northeastern Jiangxi, attempting to seize Fuzhou to threaten Nanchang. However, after Wu Qihui and Zhou Hunyuan recaptured Jinxi, and Sun Lianzhong repelled the bandit forces near Linchuan, Zhu Mao's rear was cut off, and Peng Dehuai was blocked in Nancheng and Nanfeng, unable to converge. Therefore, they retreated from Jinxi to Zixi, joining forces with Fang Shao in Guixi, reigniting their strength and recapturing Jinxi for the second time, counterattacking Xuwan. Fang Shao also attempted to invade Jinxian and Dongxiang from Guixi and Yujiang. After receiving this information, Commander-in-Chief Jiang telegraphed the Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the Jiangxi-Guangdong-Fujian border region in Nanchang, appointing Chen Cheng, commander of the 18th Army, as the front-line commander of the Fuzhou Red Army Suppression. Simultaneously, he telegraphed the 18th Army's Zhou Zhirou, the 4th Army's Wu Qihui, and the 10th Army's Li Mo'an, newly arrived from Wuhan, to concentrate in Fuzhou and advance towards Jinxi for suppression. Chen Cheng arrived in Fuzhou from Nanchang on the 1st, assuming the position of commander. In addition to the 26th Route Army's Sun Lianzhong's division firmly defending Fuzhou city with strict vigilance, the remaining divisions unanimously switched from defense to offense, searching and advancing. According to military news from Fuzhou, the 18th Army in the central route recaptured Xuwan Town, located at the junction of Linchuan and Jinxi, yesterday. Before leaving, the bandits kidnapped over seventy wealthy merchants from the town, demanding ransoms ranging from thousands to tens of thousands of yuan per person. After a brief deployment in Xuwan, the army is advancing towards Jincheng. The 4th Army on the right flank is attacking the bandits' left flank and has reached the west of Jinxi from Yiji. There are also reports of recapturing Jincheng yesterday. Zhou Hunyuan's troops on the left flank have returned to Guixi, cutting off the contact between Zhu Mao and Fang Shao. The situation in eastern Jiangxi has eased compared to before. The four main provincial roads, previously closed for military transport, have uniformly resumed operations since the 1st. As for the 10th Army's Wei Lihuang's troops and Li Mo'an's division, newly arrived in Jiangxi, they arrived in Wan at the end of last month and successively crossed the province to Fuzhou yesterday, advancing fiercely towards the front lines. The 83rd Division's Liu Kan's troops have also departed from Wuhan and will arrive shortly. The military strength in the Fu River area is over seven divisions. Mao Bingwen, Xu Kexiang, and Li Yunjie's divisions are stationed in Nancheng and Nanfeng. Zhu Mao is under attack from both front and rear and may also attempt to flee diagonally to the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui. However, the headquarters of the three provinces has ordered Zhao Guantao, Wang Jinwen, Li Yunheng, Zhou Hunyuan, Ruan Zhaochang, and other troops in northeastern Jiangxi to be on strict alert. Regarding Commander-in-Chief Jiang's arrival in Jiangxi to supervise the suppression of bandits, the Welcome Preparation Committee and various public organizations have repeatedly telegraphed Han, requesting his early arrival. Jiang replied to the provincial party department yesterday, stating that he is deeply concerned about the suffering of the Jiangxi people and will inform them of the scheduled travel date after it is confirmed. It is rumored that Jiang fears that the bandit Xu's escape to Shaanxi may lead to further spread into Xinxing Mongolia, so he is determined to fundamentally resolve the issue in the shortest time possible to avoid losing all previous efforts. Therefore, the date of his arrival in Jiangxi is still after the Third Plenary Session. As for the suppression of bandits in this province, He Guoguang is temporarily responsible for the remaining matters, except for important ones, which will be reported to Jiang and He in Nanjing by telegram. Chen Cheng is in command of the military affairs in eastern Jiangxi. However, according to another source, when Jiang travels from Wuhan to Nanjing, he may stop in Nanchang or briefly delay in Wan to personally instruct senior generals. Therefore, the provincial government has changed the location to the Science Museum to prepare Jiang's headquarters. (December 2nd)

Han Fuju Rectifies His Troops

Personally Inspects Returning Troops

Officer Promotions to Require Examinations

Jinan Communication: Han Fuju believes that military discipline is most easily corrupted during troop operations, so the troops of the Third Route Army, after the recent Liaodong battle, need to be strictly rectified to become a strong national defense force. Therefore, he personally inspected each army after their return to Jinan from the front lines, which has already been completed. The cavalry brigade of Li Xuande's troops was the last to return to Jinan and was inspected today (3rd) at Zhangzhuang. This inspection was extremely thorough, with each person, horse, and weapon carefully checked. In addition, regular examinations are held, with company commanders and below tested on three sets of calisthenics and military spirit, among other things. Those who fail are immediately dismissed. Han Fuju also believes that quality is more important than quantity, so after returning from Jiaodong, he ordered that future soldier vacancies not be filled, and the old and weak be eliminated to save on military expenses. Promotions of officers in each division and brigade must be approved by Han himself in the province through examinations. Only those who pass are allowed to be promoted. (December 3rd)

Kidnappers Demand Huge Ransom

Zhang Zizhen, a resident of Jianjiabang, Fengxian County, was kidnapped on the night of the 28th of last month. The local 5th District Security Team arrested a suspect named Ni Nan, who confessed to the location of the hostage. However, multiple searches yielded no results. It is now known that the Chen family suddenly received a letter from the kidnappers yesterday, demanding 50,000 yuan in silver within five days at the Sanjiang Temple in Taihu Dongpu, using a specific code name for contact. Otherwise, they threatened to kill the hostage. However, the Chen family is a rural farming family with no savings. Even if they sell all their property, they cannot meet this amount. Therefore, they have decided to sacrifice the hostage and have reported the original letter to the county government for thorough investigation.

Taicang

Exemption from Busy Season Tax in War Zones

For farmland affected by the disaster in the war zone, the reduction of the busy season tax has been submitted by the county government to the provincial departments for approval to alleviate the farmers' hardship. Instructions have now been received from the Department of Finance, approving the exemption of various taxes including the formal surcharges for the upper busy season of the 21st year and the provincial taxes for the winter grain tribute of the lower busy season of the 20th year. However, according to the approved original plan, it is limited to the war zone areas. The areas that have suffered losses are still not approved for exemption. The county government has ordered the Finance Bureau to revise the list and make corrections accordingly.

Jiang Wulang and Xu Nanshan, the notorious kidnappers who kidnapped Cao Runtang, Cui Liangcai, and three other merchants and civilians of this county, were brought from the Southern Tong Bandit Suppression Unit to Taicang. After multiple trials by Judge Wu Cheng, they stubbornly denied the charges. The abducted victims, including Cui Liangcai, were summoned to testify in court, and the bandits finally confessed. Yesterday, Jiang and Xu were sentenced to life imprisonment and immediately sent to prison for execution.

The outgoing district chiefs of this county have mostly not completed the handover, which not only causes difficulties for the incoming chiefs but also easily leads to corruption in public funds. The county government has established a committee to audit the handover of the district offices, appointing members from the county government's Second Section, Finance Bureau, Construction Bureau, Property Management Office, and Storage Committee to verify and calculate the public funds.

Wuxi

County Magistrate Inspects Robbery Case

The home of Zhou Jinxiang, a resident of Laowufang Village, 343rd Block, 12th District, was suddenly robbed late on the night of the 30th of last month, and his thirteen-year-old grandson, Arong, was kidnapped. The victim reported the incident to the county, requesting an investigation. County Magistrate Chen Chuande, concerned about the rampant robberies during the winter security period and the worrisome security situation, personally inspected the scene in the countryside the day before yesterday, accompanied by Police Chief Wu Zhengrong and guards. He first visited the district office of the 12th District to inspect for a week and summoned the security team for a briefing. He then walked to the scene of the incident to investigate the bandits' tracks and inquire about the kidnapping situation. He returned to the boat at dusk and took a downstream express train to Suzhou to discuss joint defense matters with the County Magistrate of Wuxian.

Gang of Bandits Rob and Injure People

During the winter security period, reports of robberies are frequent. Yesterday, news came that the home of Zhu Xianwen, a resident of Antou Lane near the Buli Xin Dyeing Factory outside the North Gate, was also robbed. Zhu is in his twilight years and is currently the director of the Suzhou-Wuxi Shipping Office and the chief of the Wuhe Township in the First District. There is only one wife and two daughters-in-law in the family. It is said that around twelve o'clock the night before, a large gang of forty to fifty bandits suddenly arrived, armed with pistols, wooden sticks, ropes, and other items. They first stationed sentries nearby, then broke down the door and rushed in, dragging Zhu's wife and others out of their beds, tying them up with ropes, burning their lower bodies with candles, and slashing their necks with kitchen knives, forcing them to reveal the location of the hidden silver. They then ransacked the boxes and cabinets, plundering at will. After about two hours, they left with their loot, including clothes, jewelry, silver coins, and other items, worth over a thousand yuan. Afterwards, neighbors untied the victims, compiled a list of losses, and reported to the county government, requesting an investigation.

Yangzhou

Conflict Between Finance and Education Chiefs

The Jiangdu government has seen a significant decrease in revenue since the autumn floods. Therefore, the various agencies that draw funds from local taxes have been subject to repeated cuts, and many are unable to receive their payments on time. Among them, the education funds have been in the most arrears. Director Xu of the Education Bureau, feeling deeply the difficulty of funding, has repeatedly settled accounts with the Finance Bureau. The Education Bureau believes that the funds that should have been received are often diverted by the Finance Bureau for other purposes. The two directors have had a major conflict, and Director Xu resigned and went to the province yesterday (4th). The local authorities have repeatedly tried to persuade him to stay and promised to order the county to strictly order the Finance Bureau to properly allocate funds to maintain education. After hearing the news, the teachers publicly elected Zhou Yu, the principal of the Eastern District Elementary School, to lead the charge in sending a telegram to the Education Department, urging Xu to stay and requesting strict pursuit of the arrears. This morning, the principals of the elementary schools in the Central District gathered at the Mashan Temple for an emergency meeting. At 10 a.m., they met with County Magistrate Ma, requesting him to strictly order the Finance Bureau chief to stop diverting education funds and to send personnel to the bureau to settle the diverted education funds for several months. Each teacher will hand over the outstanding payments as soon as possible.

Reducing the Price of Salt Permits

The transportation and sale of salt along the four banks of the Yangtze River belonging to Hunan, Hubei, West Anhui, and Anhui involves numerous items and a huge amount. The prices of permits vary from bank to bank and are all included in the selling price, causing the people to suffer greatly. The Salt Inspection Office, in order to reorganize tax revenue and reduce the burden on salt consumers, has issued a special order to eliminate all bad practices to prevent embezzlement and ordered the salt offices of the four banks to properly handle the reduction of the permit price for salt merchants. The Anhui bank has already reduced the price by four cents per unit according to the ratio. The price of each stone of salt from north to south Anhui is twelve yuan and four cents. The price of each stone in Lai, Lai, Quan, and three counties is set at nine yuan and four jiao, which has been announced to the various banks for implementation.

Zhenjiang

Assassination Case in Gaozi Town

Luo Jiade, a farmer from Henan who lived near Zhangjiazhuang, Wugang, Gaozi, was over forty years old. One day recently at 8 p.m., during dinner, two people knocked on the door of Luo's house, saying they wanted to go to Ji'an Nunnery but were lost. They asked Luo to lead the way. Luo saw that they were acquaintances and led them. Luo's wife followed her husband, but after walking a few steps, two more people came from the side and strangled Luo to death with a rope. One of them said to Luo's wife, "You can find your husband tomorrow at Cao Mang Mountain." Luo's wife, because it was dark and out of familial affection, originally wanted to call for help, but fearing that she would be harmed by the large number of people, she did not make a sound. The next day, Luo's wife went to the address and found her husband's body in the mountain's stream. She hired someone to retrieve the body. A small millstone was tied to his chest, a very tragic sight. Luo's wife has buried her husband and reported the situation to the district chief, requesting justice.

Fenghsiang Restaurant to Reopen

The Zhenjiang Fenghsiang Silver Company was burned down by a fire caused by a short circuit in the electric lights a month ago. However, due to the economic depression and thinking that it would be difficult for the employees to make a living, he changed his mind and decided to continue fighting. He has reached an agreement with the landlord and has started rebuilding. The work should be completed within the year, and the business can be reopened in the new year.

Transoceanic Telephone Call Between China and Italy

Iron, Times, Zeng Zhongming, Italian Envoy, Ciano, etc.

Met with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini the night before last

New equipment on the Italian ship Conte Russo

The Da Bai News Agency reports: The Italian postal ship Conte Russo has the world's latest invention, a long-distance telephone device. It is as if one is in the same room, no matter how far away. When the ship arrived in Shanghai last time, it was tested by the Italian Minister to China, Mr. Ciano, who spoke with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. The result was exceptionally satisfactory. The ship travels between Shanghai and Italy and is the most luxurious postal ship in the world. It is also very fast, taking only 23 days for a one-way trip to Europe, which is more than one-third shorter than ordinary postal ships. The ship arrived in Shanghai from Europe the day before yesterday and is berthed at the No. 11 floating buoy in Yangshupu. Mr. Ciano specially telegraphed to Beijing, inviting Tie Times and Zeng Zhongming to Shanghai for testing to prepare for commercial use. Mr. Zeng arrived in Shanghai from Beijing the day before yesterday. At 11:30 PM the night before last (the 4th) (4:30 PM Rome time), Mr. and Mrs. Ciano, together with Mr. Zeng, boarded the ship and spoke with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Italian Minister of Transportation Ciano, and the Chinese Chargé d'affaires to Italy. The sound waves were exceptionally clear. The situation at the time is recorded below:

Equipment on the Ship: Of the postal ships with long-distance telephone devices, there are only three in the world, two American and one Italian. The American ships travel between Europe and America, and the only Italian ship traveling between Europe and Asia is the Conte Russo. This time, the wireless radio room is divided into two rooms, located on the highest deck of the ship, one at the bow and one in the midship, each with several people in charge. The radio station in Italy is located within the Italian Ministry of Transportation. Any telephone call from the ship can be received there and then transferred to an ordinary city telephone and connected to the home of the person who wishes to speak. There is no distance that cannot be reached in England, Italy, Germany, and France.

Telephone Conversation: Italian Minister of Transportation Ciano is the father of Italian Minister Ciano, so after the call was made from the ship, it was received at Mr. Ciano's home. However, when Mr. Ciano identified himself as Ciano of Shanghai, his family suspected it was nonsense and hung up. The call was made again, and Mr. Ciano's father personally answered the call. After the introduction, Zeng Zhongming spoke with Mr. Ciano, first thanking him for the call and hoping that the friendship between the two countries would be strengthened. Mr. Ciano said that Prime Minister Mussolini was very willing to talk with him but was unfortunately out on official business, which was deeply regrettable. Then he spoke with Liu, the Chargé d'affaires at the Chinese Embassy in Italy, for a long time. At about 12:00 (5:00 PM Rome time), the Italian radio station said that the Prime Minister had already returned home. The Italian Minister's wife, who is Mussolini's daughter, answered the call first, chatting about family matters in a very affectionate manner. Then Mr. Zeng answered the call, first expressing his respect to Mr. Mussolini. Mr. Mussolini also wished our China prosperity. The conversation ended at 2:00 AM (7:00 PM Rome time). The reporter from the Da Bai News Agency also listened carefully during the call, and the words were very clear, even more so than the long-distance line between Beijing and Shanghai. Telephone Rates: The ship has already successfully tested this wireless telephone and has decided to open it for public use. When the ship arrives at the port, one can go directly to the ship to make a call, whether to a private residence, government office, or business in Europe or Southeast Asia. The price is 25 yuan (in national currency) per three minutes for Italy, 31 yuan for Australia, 41 yuan for Belgium, 35 yuan for France, 35 yuan for Germany, and 30 yuan for Switzerland.

The Japanese Arrest of Jin Cheol Contains Unfathomable Intentions

▲ Special Attention was Paid to Sino-Korean Relations During the Interrogation

▲ Jin Leaves Shanghai for Medical Treatment, Entrusting Wu Kaisheng to Handle Negotiations

The New Sound News Agency reports that after the Municipal Government protested to the French and Japanese Consulates over the case of the Japanese sending people to break into the French Concession to arrest people without authorization, both sides are now considering it. However, the Japanese's assistance in illegally arresting Jin Yongdohk contains other intentions. Jin has now left Shanghai for medical treatment, and all negotiations have been entrusted to lawyer Wu Kaisheng. The property confiscated by the Japanese when he was arrested the other day has been requested by lawyer Cai Xiaobai from the French Consulate in a letter yesterday to be recovered from the Japanese side. The details are recorded below:

Jin Cheol and Jin Cheol Left Shanghai: After Jin Cheol was released from the French Consulate, he resided at Room 606, 6th floor, Dahuh Hotel, Dongxinqiao, under the alias Liao, and asked a famous doctor from the Red Cross to treat him. The injuries from being tied up on his hands and feet had not yet recovered. His left side of his back was bruised, and his chest was also swollen. According to the doctor's examination, his lungs were injured due to being violently struck while struggling. There was a scratch on the right side of his nose, and three blows to the back of his head. His hands and feet were numb and he could barely hold a pen. His hair was combed halfway, and several strands were pulled out, with traces of blood. At 8:30 AM on the 4th, a certain Chinese gentleman sent him to Nanxiang by car. His son Jin Cheol went with him. Jin Cheol suffered more than fifty injuries on his head, hands, feet, and body due to fighting with Japanese detectives. His mouth was stuffed with a towel by the Japanese detectives several times, causing his skin to break and bleed, making it difficult for him to eat. According to the doctor, his life is not in danger.

The Japanese's Intentions in Arresting Jin: After Jin's friends sent Jin off, they visited the reporter yesterday after being entrusted by Jin to talk about the Japanese side's intention during the interrogation of Jin Yongdohk. It is said that the main points of interest are roughly as follows: 1) Asking about the source of Jin's finances when he served as the Minister of Finance of the Korean Revolutionary Party, from which Chinese agency and from whom did it come, and from which place and whom in Korea was it sent; 2) How was the military organization of the Korean Revolutionary Party, how was the source of military pay and the supply of munitions, and who and which agency in China provided assistance, and in what amount; 3) Who were the Chinese people he associated with in Shanghai, and who were the important people in the Shanghai Korean Revolutionary Party's agency? There were many other matters, but none involved the word "China." Jin replied that there was no such thing, and was therefore beaten.

Recovering Confiscated Property: The French and Japanese Consulates have reportedly received the Municipal Government's protest but have not yet given a formal response. Both sides are still studying it. However, Cai Xiaobai, Jin's representative lawyer, believes that the Japanese's confiscation of Jin's property is unreasonable and sent a letter to the French Consulate in his capacity as a representative yesterday afternoon, requesting that it be recovered from the Japanese side. The content of the letter stated that Jin Yongdohk was kidnapped by the Japanese side, and after being released through the negotiations of your consulate, this lawyer represents Jin Yongdohk in expressing his gratitude. However, Jin had $560 in silver dollars, a gold watch, a fountain pen, a stamp, and a呢大衣with him when he was arrested. In addition to requesting the Municipal Government to negotiate, I am sending this letter to your Consul-General to request that it be recovered from the Japanese side.

Huang Zhanying's History: Jin's arrest was entirely due to the machinations of the traitor Huang Zhanying. Huang is from Taishan County, Guangdong, and is about thirty years old. He followed Central Committee member Li Liejun for many years and worked in lawyer Wu Chengyu's office for a long time, and had many connections with revolutionary party members from Guangdong. This time, he met Jin Cheol through the introduction of a certain gentleman from Guangdong, but unexpectedly, he committed this act of betraying his country and his friends. After Jin Cheol was kidnapped, the police searched Huang's residence and removed all his name cards, documents, and suitcases, leaving only wooden furniture and bedding, which shows how deeply premeditated it was. Huang rented a building across from the Shanghai Bank on Avenue Joffre this summer and lived there for several months before moving to No. 2 Ruyili, Avenue du Roi Albert, to set up his office.

Hiring Lawyer Wu Kaisheng: After Jin Cheol was arrested, lawyer Cai Xiaobai of the Wu Kaisheng Law Firm was introduced by a certain gentleman to handle the case. Because the case involved the legal rights of China and France, Wu Kaisheng was also introduced by a certain gentleman to handle the case. According to lawyer Wu's remarks, the illegal arrest of Korean resident Jin Yongdohk by Japanese police in China was handled by lawyer Cai Xiaobai of this law firm. Thanks to the Municipal Government and the French Consul-General's legal struggle, a satisfactory result was obtained, and the people of the country are grateful and gratified. This is the second illegal action by the Japanese since the arrest of political prisoner Ahn Chang-ho, and it has a great impact on the safety of residents of the French Concession. I sincerely hope that the French Concession will seriously negotiate with the Japanese side to prevent similar incidents from happening again in the future. However, from a legal point of view, it is still necessary to explain that Jin Yongdohk obtained Chinese nationality in October of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China and resided in the French Concession within the territory of China. Even if there is a suspicion of a crime, according to the current treaty, the Japanese Consul may request the French Consul to send him to the Special District Court for handling. Even if it is recognized that Jin Yongdohk still has Japanese nationality, he can only request extradition from the French Consul. If it is found that he has obtained Chinese nationality or is a political prisoner, the French Consul may refuse extradition. The Japanese police have absolutely no reason to arrest him themselves. Japan claims to be a civilized country, but its actions often overstep the line, which is very regrettable.

Commercial Shares Received by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

▲ 1,004 Shares Received on the 3rd

▲ The Initial Purpose Will Not Be Changed Due to the Change in the Legal Rights Association

The Guowen News Agency reports that the Ministry ordered that the commercial shares of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company be nationalized at 50 taels per share, and since the 1st of this month, the Central Bank has been handling it and reporting the number of shares received each day to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The number of shares received each day is of concern to those who care about current affairs. The reporter inquired at the current affairs meeting of the company yesterday and was received by General Manager Liu Hongsheng, who was asked about the commercial shares and the reorganization plan. According to him, the company's reform is currently under way, with each department drafting the facts that should be promoted and reformed, and then gathering various opinions to draft a reform plan. It will take three months for everything to be decided and implemented, so it is still in the planning stage at this time. As for the loan agreement signed with the China Business Corporation in the past, although I have discussed it with the other party, it is still under study. Whether the contract exists or is abolished must be inquired of the Business Corporation, and I have no way to express my opinion. Regarding the nationalization of commercial shares, 14 shares were received on the 1st of this month, 224 shares were received on the 2nd, and 666 shares were received on the 3rd, for a total of 1,004 shares. It is said that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company issued more than 40,000 shares in the past, and today it is only one-fortieth. Based on the current situation, it may be more active every day in the future. Since I took office, I have not brought money to advance, and the Board of Directors has not advanced money. The Debt Committee will be established, and the total amount owed is about 17 million, but the detailed situation must be inquired of the responsible personnel of the Committee.

The Central News Agency reports that Zhu Jia-hua, Minister of Communications, visited Song Daiyuan, President of the National Academy of Peking, at Qiqi Road yesterday afternoon at approximately 3:00 PM and did not leave until 5:00 PM. According to Minister Zhu, the government has not yet decided on its attitude towards the shareholders' Legal Rights Maintenance Association organized by some shareholders of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, but the government will not change its initial intention to nationalize the company, and the establishment of the association is not expected to have a significant impact.

A telegram from Beijing stated that Gao Tingzi, Director of the Navigation Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications, said that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company borrowed 5 million from HSBC in the twelfth year of the Republic of China, and with interest compounded, it has reached more than 7.007 million. It is difficult to thoroughly reorganize it without repaying the old debt. Now that the national treasury is tight, it is unable to raise this huge amount of money, so after the Debt Consolidation Committee is established, it will plan to borrow new funds from the banking sector to repay the old debts through legal procedures in order to gradually reform.

The Local Court Will Issue a Warrant to Arrest Chen Fumu

A certain important official of the Ministry of Communications told the Xinshi News Agency reporter yesterday that Chen Fumu, the former director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, embezzled money and committed fraud. The local court has repeatedly issued summonses, but Chen has failed to appear in court. Now the court has decided to file a public prosecution and issue a warrant to arrest Chen to ensure that he is brought to justice and dealt with according to the law.

The Japanese Navy Ministry Has Sent an Additional Squadron of Warships to Shanghai

▲ The 27th Squadron, Three Ships Arrived. The Japanese Navy Ministry will reorganize the 3rd Fleet stationed in Shanghai. In addition to designating the flagship Izumo and the cruiser Tenryu, it will also transfer the 27th Destroyer Squadron of four ships from the Yokosuka Naval Base to Shanghai to join the 3rd Fleet. The squadron left Japan on the 4th, and three of the ships sailed to Shanghai yesterday, arriving at Woosung at noon and sailing into the Huangpu River in the afternoon to anchor on the Yangshupu river.

▲ The New Commander Will Arrive in Shanghai Soon. The newly appointed Commander of the 3rd Fleet, Rear Admiral Yonai, has been ordered to come to Shanghai from Sasebo to take office. Yonai has already left Sasebo for Shanghai aboard the flagship Izumo, leading the 27th Destroyer Squadron. According to a message from the Japanese Naval Headquarters in this port, if Yonai does not arrive in Shanghai today, he will definitely arrive tomorrow morning. Japanese naval officers in Shanghai, such as Commander Sakano, have prepared to welcome the new commander.

▲ Sugioka Visits Mayor Wu. At 11:00 AM yesterday, Rear Admiral Sugioka, Commander of the Japanese Naval Landing Force in Shanghai, accompanied by his adjutant Onuma, visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government to thank him for his congratulations on Sugioka's promotion to Rear Admiral. Sugioka and Mayor Wu talked for about 40 minutes before leaving. At noon, Mayor Wu hosted a banquet at his private residence for Colonel Shima, Lieutenant Colonel Higuchi, Sakai, Kamata, and other two lieutenant colonels of the Japanese Naval Landing Force to bid farewell to the officers who were returning home after being promoted.

▲ Two Ship Captains Arrive in Shanghai. Tadashi Sawa, the newly appointed captain of the Japanese Navy ship Atami on the Yangtze River, and Eiji Matsuura, captain of the Tsurumi, as well as senior officers of the landing force, Shinpei Asano and Yuzuru Tagai, were ordered by the Japanese to come to Shanghai to take over their positions and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Because the Atami and other ships are upstream on the Yangtze River, Sawa and others are scheduled to take the Nisshin Maru to Hankou today to take over their positions.
