Electric Silk Weaving Factory Industry Requests Refund of Rayon Import Tax

The Shanghai Electric Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association, considering the severe impact on the export sales of silk fabrics, previously sent a letter to the International Trade Association, forwarding it to the Ministry of Finance, requesting a refund of the rayon import tax, as reported in previous newspapers. Two months have passed since then, but it has not been implemented. In order to promote the development of international trade, the association is eager to find a solution. Now, they have prepared a summary and plan to send representatives to visit Minister of Finance Song to personally explain the situation and request the prompt refund of the rayon import tax to reduce costs and provide relief. The original text of the summary is copied below:

Summary:

Due to the Ministry of Finance's additional rayon tax imposed on August 4th, the export trade of rayon fabrics and rayon-mixed fabrics woven by domestic silk factories to foreign countries such as Southeast Asia and India has been greatly affected. It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance refund the collected rayon tax at the original rates for all rayon fabrics woven by domestic factories and exported to foreign trade, in order to alleviate the distress of the domestic silk weaving industry and promote the development of foreign trade. The impact, process, measures, and benefits of this matter are listed below to prove that it will not affect national tax revenue, but merchants will benefit immensely.

(1) Impact:

The increase in the rayon tax was originally intended to alleviate the decline in the price of domestic natural silk. However, after implementation, not only has the domestic silk market not seen any effective results, but the domestic silk weaving industry has been severely impacted in markets such as Southeast Asia and India. The rayon tax was first imposed in 1931. At that time, the sales of Chinese silk in Southeast Asia and India suffered a significant decline. A table is provided below for comparison:

Comparison of Chinese Silk Sales in Southeast Asia

| Year | 1929 | 1931 |

| ------ | ----------- | ----------- |

| Location | Sales Value | Sales Value |

| India | 8 million taels | 5 million taels |

| Annam | 5 million taels | 2 million taels |

| Singapore | 5 million taels | 2 million taels |

According to the silver amounts listed in the table, rayon-mixed fabrics and rayon fabrics account for 60-70%. After China increased the rayon tax, the sales of Chinese silk were actually 50% lower than before the increase. The significant impact is self-evident. On August 4th of this year, the rayon import tax was increased again, by 15 customs gold units per picul, resulting in a 5% to 15% increase in the cost of rayon fabrics. Therefore, the selling price also increased. Japanese rayon fabrics, due to their low cost, have always been cheaper than Chinese silk in Southeast Asia and India. Now, they are making every effort to dump their products there. If Chinese silk also reduces its price, it will inevitably suffer significant losses. If the price is not reduced, it will be stockpiled and ignored. Business has plummeted, and foreign trade silk merchants are hesitant to move forward.

(2) Process:

Based on the above situation, the Shanghai Electric Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association sent a letter to the China International Trade Association on August 5th, stating the reasons, requesting the Ministry of Finance (Industry) to refund the originally collected rayon import tax for all rayon fabrics and rayon-mixed fabrics woven by domestic factories and exported to foreign countries, in order to reduce costs and maintain the inherent position of the silk market in India and Southeast Asia. Subsequently, the association received a reply stating that the Ministry of Industry had requested the Ministry of Finance to investigate. Two months have passed, but the Ministry of Finance has not yet approved it. As the sales of silk by domestic silk manufacturers to Southeast Asia and India are declining day by day, we request prompt approval again.

(3) Measures:

If the refund of the rayon import tax is approved, if cash is refunded, not only will the customs be cumbersome, but the procedures will also be complicated. Therefore, it is suggested that the customs specially print a type of customs gold unit voucher for the refund of the rayon import tax, fill in the amount at any time, and refund it. Any domestic factory exporting rayon fabrics for foreign trade should first register the product name and composition with the customs for record purposes, so that there is a basis for investigation and no malpractices will occur. When rayon fabrics are exported for foreign trade, the "Customs Gold Unit Voucher for Rayon Import Tax" should be issued at the time of customs declaration, allowing it to be used to fully offset the rayon import tax in the future. This is a simple and easy measure that will benefit merchants immensely.

(4) Benefits:

After the rayon import tax is refunded, on the surface, the government's tax revenue may seem slightly insufficient. However, in reality, it will not only not be reduced, but it will also increase tax revenue. Currently, after the increase in the rayon import tax, the export of rayon fabrics from domestic factories has gradually decreased, resulting in a shortfall in export tax revenue. If the refund of the rayon import tax is approved, the export sales of woven fabrics will inevitably be prosperous. Furthermore, the raw materials for these silks are half rayon and half domestic natural silk. With the vigorous export of silk, domestic silk will also have a way out. This is something that the government should encourage. Last year, the Ministry of Industry issued a plan to encourage industry, which included a special clause stating that "the raw material tax for all exported goods can be refunded upon export." Now, merchants are requesting a refund of the rayon import tax, which is not an excessive demand and seems reasonable. Moreover, it will have absolutely no impact on the government's tax revenue. As the crisis is imminent and the silk industry is on the verge of bankruptcy, we dare to request the Minister to promptly approve it in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and maintain the industry. This is a truly virtuous and convenient measure.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Electric Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association (Seal)

Zhabei Police and Defense Corps Joint Defense Meeting

Three resolutions were passed. The temporarily organized Sixth Team of the Zhabei Xibaoxing Road Hubei District Defense Corps held a joint police and defense corps meeting with the Xibaoxing Road and Baziqiao branch stations of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau at 7 PM last night. Those present included Inspector Li Jinrong of the Baoxing Road branch station of the Fifth District, Inspector Li Jianwu of the Baziqiao branch station, (Wu Deyun representing), Chen Weihan, supervisor of the Sixth Team, Wu Junfeng, captain, Li Guanyi, platoon leader, Mao Zenghuan, administrator, and more than ten other people. Chen Weihan was elected chairman, and Huang Haoyuan recorded the minutes. Chairman Chen Weihan reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating briefly that the team has been on duty for a week since receiving orders, but the responsibility of defending the country is to supplement the shortcomings of the police. During this winter defense period, it is necessary to maintain contact. Effective collaboration should be adopted for local defense. Inspector Li Jinrong said that the police and defense corps are essentially one family with no distinction between them. He expressed great sympathy for adopting a liaison approach to local defense and suggested mutual assistance in case of incidents to ensure security on both sides. Resolutions: (1) Members of the corps should patrol and jointly cooperate with the police every night. (2) Patrol teams should inspect pedestrians with suspicious behavior and take consistent action with the police. (3) In the event of an accident in the defense area, the police and defense corps should communicate with each other to assist. The meeting adjourned at 8:30 PM.

Record of Inspection of the Completed Dike Project by the National Government Flood Relief Association

Welcome in Jiujiang

The Jiangxin wheel arrived in Jiujiang at 9 pm on December 1st. Representatives from the county party headquarters, the chamber of commerce, and all walks of life arrived at the pier to welcome them. Then, Jiujiang County Magistrate Jiang Ji, accompanied by all members of the delegation, walked to the nearby Zhenxing Western Restaurant. They hosted a tea party in the name of the Jiujiang County Government. During the banquet, County Magistrate Jiang first delivered a welcome speech, stating briefly that he recalled the floods of the previous year. The people of Jiangxi Province survived in a life-and-death situation, thanks to the relief from your association. The great dike project has been built, benefiting the rural areas. On behalf of all sectors of the county, I would like to thank you. The reception is simple, and I hope you will forgive us. Li Zushi, on behalf of the inspection team, replied, stating briefly that today we appreciate that County Magistrate Jiang came to welcome us from afar, which shows his concern for the people's suffering. The Flood Relief Association will expedite the completion of the unfinished projects in Jiangxi, and we are very willing to continue to serve Jiangxi Province with our remaining efforts. On behalf of the entire inspection team, I would like to thank Mr. Jiang and representatives from all walks of life for their kind intentions. Next, representatives from the county party headquarters and the chamber of commerce gave speeches, expressing their deep welcome. Finally, Sun Faxu, a member of the inspection team, gave a speech entitled "The Model Village of China." Mr. Sun once served as the model county magistrate of Ding County, Hebei Province, and has served as the governor of Shandong and Shanxi provinces. His political achievements were well-known at the time. He was a subordinate of Li Huangpo. When Mr. Sun spoke, he used a humorous tone and contained deep meaning. He criticized those who blindly believed in Europeanization. His speech is worth recording, so it is recorded as follows: Mr. Sun said that he was able to participate in the inspection team. After resigning as the governor of Shanxi Province, he engaged in farmland planting. The land he cultivated was in Tongcheng, Anhui, where the inspection team visited. He was studying rural economic cooperation when he was suddenly hit by the worst flood in a century, which inundated all the farmland. In fact, he is a pure disaster victim. Thanks to the government's advocacy, social promotion, and donations from friendly countries, the embankment that was completely destroyed over thousands of miles up and down the Yangtze River can be restored to its original state with the least economic cost and the shortest time. This is not only difficult in China's complicated political situation, but it would not be easy to recover so quickly even if a civilized country in Europe and America encountered the above situation. For us disaster victims, our gratitude must be greater than that of ordinary people, without the need for further explanation. As a pure disaster victim, he can participate in the inspection team and spend time with philanthropists, engineering experts, and journalists from China and abroad, and follow them to inspect the dike project. Seeing the consolidation of the project, he cannot help but admire it. Tonight, he wanted to give a speech entitled "Zhaicheng Model Village, Ding County, Hebei Province, China." He believes that there are three essential elements of politics: (1) the people must be organized; (2) the people must have the ability to govern themselves, without relying on external forces to seek progress; (3) the people must have economic knowledge, and all actions must be in line with economic principles in order to advance smoothly and prevent distorted development. Zhaicheng Model Village is located in the east of the county, 30 miles from the city, with about 2,000 people. Its customs are good, and the beginning of the organization focused on the aforementioned three elements. Therefore, the village has an elders association, a women's association, and a youth association. Those who are farmers and workers have the organization of agricultural and industrial associations. Roads, bridges, cleanliness, and hygiene are all based on their ability to govern themselves, without relying on external forces, so that people can see at a glance that it is a model of self-government. Secondly, all the people in the village are diligent and thrifty, and can gradually progress according to the economic strength of the whole village. Gentlemen, people often criticize that the Chinese people have no organization, no self-governing ability, and no economic knowledge. The Zhaicheng Village in Ding County, which I mentioned, can be visited by those who have visited it, and can know that this village can slightly cleanse the shame of the Chinese people. The biggest feature of this village is two: (1) The villagers are harmonious and eliminate litigation; (2) Every year, taxes are paid during a certain period, and the village chief goes to the county to pay them. If you travel to Ding County, try to consult the receipt book of the judicial organs. Zhaicheng has no civil or criminal litigation. Try to read the collection books. Zhaicheng has never been punished for arrears. This is enough to comfort Chinese and foreigners. Mr. Sun finally concluded his speech by saying that today all sectors of Jiujiang gathered here to welcome us, or it is like the story of Anqing, waiting for a long time at the pier, or even not having a full meal. I am very sorry for my lengthy speech. I should pause here. Until half past twelve, the guests and hosts parted happily and returned to Jiangxin wheel. (Qian Hua left Jiujiang at 12 pm on December 1st)

First Special Court's New President Guo Yunguan Sworn In

Guo Speaks of Shanghai's Every Variety of Prosperity

It Must Be Done So That Corruption is Eliminated and the Atmosphere is Pure

| Large Discussion on How Judges Must Not Love Money |

Guo Yunguan, the newly appointed acting president of the Shanghai First Special District Court, held a swearing-in ceremony at 3:00 PM yesterday in the Sixth Tribunal on the third floor of the new building of the court. Military, police, and political figures from various organizations in the city came to the court to witness the ceremony, and the turnout was exceptionally enthusiastic, filling the hall. The scene was quite grand. President Guo personally greeted the guests with amiability and attentiveness. The details of the event are as follows:

The Arrangement of the Auditorium: The auditorium was located in the Sixth Tribunal on the third floor of the new building on the east side of the court. A portrait of the Prime Minister and the Prime Minister's will were hung in the center, and the oath, party song, and agenda of the inauguration were posted on the left and right sides. The Party and national flags were crossed above them. The walls were covered with signs indicating the seats for the supervisor, oath-taker, party representatives, guests, and journalists. At the main entrance of the special court, a white cloth with the black characters "The World is for All" and the couplet "The Revolution is Not Yet Complete," "Comrades Still Need to Strive" were hung, along with two crossed Party and national flags. The guest registration area was set up there.

The Ceremony of the Inauguration: ㈠ The supervisor takes the chair; ㈡ The oath-taker takes their place; ㈢ The entire audience stands at attention; ㈣ The Party song is sung; ㈤ The highest respect is paid to the national flag, the Party flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister; ㈥ The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will; ㈦ Three minutes of silence; ㈧ The oath is taken; ㈨ The supervisor gives an instruction; ㈩ The Party representative delivers a speech; ㈩㈠ The guests deliver speeches; ㈩㈡ The oath-taker gives a reply; ㈩㈢ The ceremony concludes with a photograph.

Guest List: Wang Zhengting, former Minister of Foreign Affairs and Central Committee Member; Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai; Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Police Bureau; Shen Yi, Director of the Municipal Works Bureau; Wang Yiga, Representative of the Garrison Headquarters; Ying Shi, President of the Second Special District Court; Wang Xun, Representative of the Shanghai District Court; Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Xu Jiqing from the banking sector; He Dehui, Assistant of the Public Concession; Wang Yaotang, lawyer for the Public Concession; Shen Junru and Li Zuyu, representatives of the Lawyers' Association; lawyer Lin Yingqing; and all judges, prosecutors, and reporters from various newspapers and news agencies of the First Special Court, totaling more than 300 people, gathered in one place.

The President's Oath: I, Guo Yunguan, solemnly swear that I will恪遵循 the Prime Minister's will, obey the Party's principles, abide by the laws, and be loyal and diligent in my duties. I pledge never to waste a single penny, never to misuse a single person, and never to engage in self-interest, fraud, or the acceptance of bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This I swear.

The Supervisor's Instructions: Yu Hua, Presiding Judge of the Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, delivered instructions on behalf of Shen Jia, President of the court, stating, in brief: Today, President Guo is being sworn in, and I am very honored to participate in this grand ceremony on behalf of President Shen of the Second Branch of the High Court. The oath that the oath-taker has just read covers the main points of loyalty, diligence, not wasting a single penny, and not misusing a single person. It is hoped that the oath-taker will put these points into practice. As for the statement of never accepting bribes, it is especially important for judicial officials. Fortunately, President Guo has a deep understanding of this. I recall that when the Lawyers' Association hosted President Guo a few days ago, someone at the banquet asked President Guo to express his political views. President Guo said, "Governance does not require much talk." This shows that President Guo seeks practicality in all matters, and therefore, he will surely strive to uphold all points in the oath.

▲ Guest Speeches: First, Mr. Wang Zhengting took the stage to speak, stating, in brief: Today, President Guo is being sworn in, and I am very honored and pleased to have this opportunity to participate. Outsiders often feel that our country lacks specialized talent, but in fact, it is not that we lack talent, but that it is often not used in the right way. President Guo has studied both Chinese and Western systems and has a particular interest in law. He worked in the Chinese delegation to the League of Nations. After returning to China, he continued to diligently study law and can truly be regarded as a legal expert. Now, the judicial authorities have appointed President Guo to preside, which is truly using his expertise. From now on, President Guo will surely make contributions to the country and society. Law is originally a kind of writing, and its effectiveness depends entirely on the proper application of the judge. The people value law greatly and respect the court because they believe that law can protect life and property. It is impossible to express in words the joy of having a president who is so knowledgeable and deeply studied in law. Although our country has now achieved tariff autonomy, the consular jurisdiction has not yet been abolished. Although this is the responsibility of the diplomatic authorities, all countries are paying attention to whether our country's judges can be dedicated and law-abiding. President Guo is already dedicated and will surely be an aid to diplomacy in the future, allowing all countries to understand that our country not only reforms the law but also has good judges. Then, Wang Yiga, representative of the Garrison Headquarters, and Shen Junru, representative of the Lawyers' Association, delivered speeches in succession. The speeches were lengthy, so details are omitted.

▲ President Guo's Reply: Today, Yunguan is being sworn in, and I am deeply grateful for your presence and guidance. This court was created based on an agreement, and Minister Wang was the one who signed the agreement. Minister Wang said just now that complete recovery cannot be achieved with empty words. This is because although our country's laws are gradually improving, it is also necessary to have people who govern the laws. Yunguan has always advocated not indulging in empty talk but seeking practical implementation. Therefore, there is nothing that can be expressed at present. As for the meaning of the oath, to summarize, it means not to love money. The country knows that the power of money is great, so it repeatedly reminds officials when they take office. There is a saying that military officials are not afraid of death, and civil officials do not love money. Especially judges must not love money. Shanghai is full of prosperity, so people must have a firm heart so as not to be swayed by customs. An ancient sage said, "If you are determined to eat vegetable roots, there is nothing difficult in the world." Saying you don't want money, but then being unwilling to let go when money comes to the door, depends on one's usual cultivation. Yunguan has never liked socializing. When I arrived in Shanghai a few days ago, because I had to host a banquet, I specially chose the "Vegetable Root Fragrance" restaurant on Sanma Road. During the banquet, I made a very solemn statement. Although today is Yunguan's swearing-in, this oath applies to all colleagues. I only hope that we will work together to eliminate corruption and create a pure atmosphere. I hope that all sectors will not hesitate to give advice and give us spiritual assistance.

Small Business is Not Easy

Westerners in the Health Department Deliberately Make Things Difficult

Newly Opened Snack Shop Cannot Cope

The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Secretary of the Public Concession yesterday, stating: Dear Sir, According to a letter from Feng Xiren, I have opened a snack shop at 43389 Roberts Road in Xinxishi. Before opening, on September 10th, I applied to the Public Concession to obtain a food shop license. Staff from the Fire Brigade, Works Bureau, and Health Department came to inspect. According to the staff at the license application office, the Fire Brigade and Works Bureau have already signed their approval, but the staff from the Health Department have not yet signed, so the license cannot be issued. I rely on this business to make a living and cannot afford to wait any longer. According to general practice, I started business in early October. I have followed all the orders of the Health Department inspector, a Westerner named Feng Shan (transliteration). According to the order of the Fire Brigade inspector, I installed the back door in the location he indicated, but Feng Shan wanted me to move it to another location, so I complied and reinstalled it. I also complied with his order to build several cement walls in the shop, building them and then being ordered to demolish them, demolishing them and then being ordered to build them again. This has already cost about 200 yuan. There was originally a water faucet and a large cement basin on the right side of the building, but I also demolished them according to Feng Shan's order. I complied with his order to reinstall a water faucet and a white porcelain basin in the shop. Now he is ordering me to reinstall the cement basin and water pipe in the original location of the water faucet and cement basin, and it must be installed in the wall. If it is not installed in the wall, it is not hygienic. He said he would come to inspect next week. Yesterday (November 29th), the First Special District Court suddenly sent a summons, stating that I had opened a food shop without obtaining a license from the Public Concession, which is a violation of regulations, and that I must appear in court at 2:00 PM on December 2nd for questioning. Therefore, I am writing to request your association's assistance so that I can make a living and avoid starvation for my family. I would be extremely grateful. After investigating, if the case is as stated in the letter, Feng Shan's behavior is close to deliberately making things difficult for people or hoping to obtain a commission for issuing a license. This kind of tripartite division of power is truly confusing. Last year, due to a certain incident, your bureau intended to find ways to improve, unify authority, and facilitate commerce. To this day, there are still such confusing situations, and there is a need for rapid improvement. In view of the aforementioned situation, we are writing to request your bureau to promptly investigate and issue the license and unify the methods to facilitate commerce.

Jealousy Leads to Bloodshed

Russian Man Hates Wife's Affair

Breaks into Room at Midnight, Uses Gun and Knife

The Da Mei Evening News reported that yesterday morning (the 4th), Li Weizi Ji, a Russian member of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps, shot and wounded Nidu Wenkefu, his wife's lover, at 51, Lane 103, Xuehuali Road, and stabbed his wife with a bayonet. Li is currently being detained at the French Concession Police Headquarters and will be transferred to the Second Special District Court for trial on Thursday. Li's wife is only 22 years old. She was wounded mostly in both arms, but her injuries are minor. After being bandaged at the hospital, she went home. Her lover, Nidu Wenkefu, was seriously injured and is currently in the Guangci Hospital. It was reported this afternoon (the 5th) that he is in critical condition. Therefore, the French police will observe Nidu's injuries for several days before prosecuting Li Weizi Ji. It is reported that Li married in Harbin in April two years ago. His wife came to Shanghai last September and soon joined the Fourth Company of the Russian Regiment of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps. His wife worked as a hostess. They lived together until two months ago, when Li's wife suddenly abandoned her husband and fell in love with a young Russian man named Nidu Wenkefu. Therefore, Li Weizi Ji wanted to get rid of Nidu. At 11:00 PM last Saturday night, after returning to the Tangshan Road barracks, he sneaked out at about 2:00 AM, carrying a gun, a bayonet, and several bullets, and went straight to Xuehuali Road. He entered the room where his wife and lover were living, shot and wounded Nidu. His wife came out to fight him, and he stabbed her several times with a bayonet. People who lived together heard the noise and came to see what was happening. They took Li's gun away. Then the police arrived and took him to the police station.

Male Corpse in Empty Coffin

▲ Baton Wounds Verified on Waist

▲ Obviously Body Dumped After Death

A male corpse was found in an empty coffin at the head of Qitu Lane, Yangsi Bridge, Pudong. It was glimpsed by the landlord Xia Haigen, and the corpse was identified by the relatives as the elderly Hu Rongjing. This has been reported previously. It is now known that the deceased was 68 years old this year and had a son who was prodigal and wandered outside all year round, and his whereabouts are unknown. The deceased also had no occupation, no production, and often depended on his nephew Zhang Guixiang (adopted by the Zhang family) for living expenses, and also borrowed money from his sister-in-law Hu Liu and others to make a living. He was a useless person. After the case was reported by the local security officer and verified, yesterday the local court appointed Prosecutor Zhang and Verification Officer Xuan to cross the river to Pudong. They verified that the deceased died due to injury, and there were baton wounds on his waist, which was obviously a planned murder and then dumped into the coffin. When questioned, Hu Liu stated that she lived at 36 Xiangqiao Lane, Dadongmen, and the deceased was her husband's brother. Before the 24th of last month, the deceased came to borrow money, but it was inconvenient, so she sent the money to Pudong on the 24th. Unexpectedly, the neighbors said that the deceased had been out for half a month and his whereabouts were unknown. After inquiring everywhere, her nephew Zhang Guixiang found the corpse in the empty coffin on the second day. Zhang Guixiang testified that he lived in Qitu. After his uncle was missing, his mother Hu Liu came and they went to various relatives to inquire, but there was no result. Later, he heard people say that a corpse was found in an empty coffin in Qitu on the 28th. At first, he saw a pair of rush shoes feet at the mouth of the empty coffin, so he recognized his uncle. The official ordered them to collect the body and perform the funeral, and because the case was bizarre, Hu Liu and Zhang Guixiang were handed over to the police station for bail, pending investigation and verification.

It is now known that the High Court has scheduled a retrial for 1:00 PM on the 14th of this month and has issued summonses to Xia Guoxin, Wang Jisheng, Wang Bujing, and the victim Yu Ti. Yun's defense lawyers are still Zhao Chen, Li Zuyu, and Shen Junru.

Pu Zhaozhao River Urgently Measuring Earthwork to Start Construction

▲ Agriculture and Shipping Both Benefit

▲ Budgeted Costs 130,000 Yuan

The Pu Zhaozhao River in West Shanghai has been in disrepair for many years. The riverbed is silted up, and the agricultural irrigation along the river has been greatly affected. In recent years, local people have been running around calling for dredging, but it has been difficult to raise funds, and the project has been delayed until now. The river enters the Huangpu River from the Rihui Port in the east, flows through Shangsong and Qingjing, and connects to the Liuhe Rihui Port in the west. The section to Xujiahui is called Zhaojia浜, and the section west of Xujiahui is called Puhuitang. The Shanghai Municipal Government, in view of the importance of the river, allocated funds for repairs, and the local people were overjoyed. It is now known that the Municipal Works Bureau has completed the planning. The Zhaojia浜 section, with its many factories on the south bank, will use dredging machines to deepen it, so as to dredge sewage. The Puhuitang west of Xujiahui will be dredged manually, and a sluice gate will be set up at the Pailou Bay to prevent sewage from Zhaojia浜 from entering. That is, at that place, according to the old Puhuitang river line, it will be opened to Caojing District from Xiaozha, connecting Caohejing Port, and exiting Baibuqiao Port to the east, so that clean water from the Huangpu River can flow into the interior. This plan is said to be perfect for agricultural irrigation and drinking water for residents. Deepening the Zhaojia浜 section will also facilitate the transportation of ships in the future, and factories will benefit even more. Due to the sudden urgency of time, it was decided to build a dam and start construction this winter, in order to complete it before the spring farming season next year. The Caojing District Municipal Committee Office has sent personnel to measure the earthwork for days. Except for the Zhaojia浜 Xiaozha section, the section to Caohejing is equivalent to opening a river in the field. The total amount of earthwork from Caohejing Port via Longhua to Baibu is estimated at more than 120,000 cubic meters. The budget for building a dam and water leakage, together with the river opening fee, requires about 130,000 yuan.

▲ Translated and Printed in English, German, and French

▲ Distributed to Europeans and Americans to Facilitate Guidance

Recently, the Ministry of Railways, because European travelers to China are not very clear about the railway routes and conditions in our country, telegraphed the Beijing-Shanghai, Hangzhou-Ningbo, Pinghan, and Jinpu railway bureaus and committees, ordering them to investigate and report in detail the general situation of each railway, railway stations, historical sites and scenic spots, important travel information, and timetables. Two Yangtze River Vessels Run Aground

▲ Baota Island Fuyang Runs Aground. The Shangjiang ship Fuyang of the Sanbei Company was chartered by the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to travel between Nanjing and Yichang. This time, sailing upstream from Beijing, on the 3rd of this month, it sailed to the Yangtze River surface of Baota Island downstream of Shashi. It encountered a retreat of upstream water, and the ship mistakenly entered a shoal and ran aground. The ship has lost its ability to move and urgently sent a telegram for help. Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau received a report and telegraphed the Hankou branch, ordering it to send a ship to tow it. The armed comrades in the ship will be transferred to Yichang by barge.

▲ Tunan is Stranded in Dongliu. The Zhaoshangju Tunan ship was also requisitioned by the military and traveled between Beijing and Hankou. On the night of the 4th of this month, when the ship sailed to the Dongliu River surface opposite Anqing, due to a mistake by the pilot, the ship ran aground in a sandbar. Repeated attempts to reverse the engine failed to dislodge it. Yesterday, it sent an urgent telegram to Shanghai for help. The Shanghai Bureau received a report and telegraphed the Yangtze River ships going upstream and downstream of the bureau to quickly go to tow it.

Activities of the National Socialist Faction

▲ Distributing Leaflets on the Fourth Floor of the East Asia Hotel

▲ Three Detainees are All University Students

At 3:50 PM on the 3rd of this month, a burst of firecrackers was suddenly heard near Nanjing Road and Zhejiang Road, followed by the sight of various colored leaflets flying in the air. At that time, some people shouted reactionary slogans. The Chinese and foreign detectives of the Laozha Police Station were dispatched to prevent and control the situation and began to arrest the people who were distributing the leaflets. Jiang Jing from Yixing, Yan Bingyuan from Jiangbei, Hou Dan from Tongzhou, and Yang Rong from Sichuan were arrested. A large five-colored flag and a large banner were found in a Happy Paradise Teahouse and taken to the police station. It was found that the leaflets were distributed from top to bottom from room 403 of the East Asia Hotel. The police chief ordered an investigation and determined that the occupants of the room were strongly suspected of being involved in the incident. The three occupants of the room, Wu Zhigao, Xie Qingyi, and Zhang Xiwei from Nanjing, were arrested and a reactionary leaflet was found on Wu. They were taken back to the police station. It was found that the detainees were all university students. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Branch of the High Court and interrogated by Judge Guo Huaipu. Li Zhishan, the police station's lawyer, stated that the police station was prosecuting in accordance with Articles 2, 62 of the Emergency Punishment Law for Endangering the Republic of China and Article 160 of the Criminal Law. It was found that the defendants were all members of the National Socialist Youth Party, with the goal of a five-ethnic republic, but they expressed dissatisfaction with the current government. The 2nd of the month was the ninth anniversary of their party, so they made a major publicity campaign the next day, which led to their arrest. The leaflets and banners were presented to the court. Judge Guo interrogated the defendants and ordered a retrial at a later date.

Wife Unable to Make a Living After Husband Takes Concubine

Pawned and Borrowed Until at the End of Her Rope

Divorce Requested, Reconciliation Hopeless

| Now Submitting Another Statement to Court Urging Trial |

Qi Zhulian, a woman from Yuyao, is 44 years old. In her youth, she married Xie Duanqin, a prominent family in the same town, through a matchmaker. She gave birth to a son who died young. After Xie took a concubine in Shanghai, he abandoned her. Initially, she relied on a nunnery, and then moved to a small house outside, relying only on pawning and borrowing to maintain her food and clothing. Recently, she has reached the end of her rope and has no way to live. She had no choice but to retain lawyer Lu Ming to file a lawsuit against her husband in the First Special District Court, requesting that a divorce be granted and that the defendant pay the original alimony of 15,000 yuan. The case was heard in September. After the lawyers for both parties completed their arguments, the judge advised the two parties to go out and reconcile first. However, two months have passed since then, and the defendant has shown no sincerity in reconciliation. It is heard that Qi has now also retained lawyer Jiang Qishi to assist lawyer Lu Dingming in submitting another statement urging trial.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Train Adds Shifts and Changes Times

▲ Implemented from December 15th

In order to facilitate passengers, the traffic department of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway has slightly modified the departure times of various passenger trains and added a Hangzhou-Jiaxing regional passenger train between Zhakou and Jiaxing, one round trip. Two freight trains have been added between Hangzhou and Shanghai. This has been discussed and decided by the traffic conference and submitted to the ministry for approval. It was originally planned to start operating on the 1st of this month, but due to the modification of the timetable and the preparation of procedures such as the allocation of locomotives and vehicles, it was decided to implement it uniformly from the 15th of this month. The timetable is currently being printed.

Pig Boat Leaks, Pigs Float on Sea

▲ Two Boat Crews Missing

He Chunyuan, a pig vendor from Jiangbei, recently invested in collecting more than 200 pigs with others in Jiangbei and hired Cheng Baorong's boat to transport them to Shanghai for sale. He and others took Cheng's boat together. On the afternoon of the previous day, while sailing outside Chongming, Cheng's boat's bottom was leaking. He kept sailing quickly, but the impact of the waves caused the boat to shake, and the damage to the seams of the boat became even greater. The boat gradually filled with water, and everyone panicked and shouted for help. A fishing boat heard the shouts and came to rescue them. The water in the boat had flooded the deck. The people in the boat were rescued, but there was no way to tow the boat. It drifted eastward and sank. The pigs that were loaded were floating all over the sea. It is said that there were two people who had invested in the sale with He and two boat crews who are missing. The loss is not small.

Manufacturing Red Pills and Counterfeit Medicines

▲ In addition to a Fine of Five Hundred Yuan

Detectives Tao Desheng, Lu Zhaolin, and Bao Jinrong of the French Concession Police, on October 29th, cracked down on a clandestine operation manufacturing red pills at a three-story building located at No. 1, Lane 3, Avenue Paul Brunat. They apprehended Zhao Qingchao, who was allegedly engaged in the illicit production, along with suspects Hu Jizhong, Wu Acheng, Ruan Agen, and four others. Confiscated were red pills, raw medicinal powder, pill-making equipment, and counterfeit medicines, including "Yan Doctor's Red Tonic Pills" and "Bianxianglu Ji Banxia." They were handed over to the Second Special District Court for public prosecution. The Lao Jin Long Foreign Firm, which managed the Red Tonic Pills, and Bianxianglu, upon learning of this, also sent representatives to the court to join the prosecution. After receiving instructions to chemically test the medicinal powder and completing the interrogation, Judge Li Changnian presided over the trial yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. Zhao Qingchao was sentenced to a fine of five hundred yuan for selling counterfeit trademarked medicines and a fine of three hundred yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia, totaling six hundred yuan in fines. Hu Jizhong, Wu Acheng, and Ruan Agen were all found not guilty.

Zhejiang Industrial Bank Inspection Report

▲ Thirtieth Time

The issuance and business operations of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank are completely separate, with ample reserves. On the 5th of this month, accountant Yan Ouning conducted an inspection and found that cash reserves accounted for over 60%, and guaranteed reserves accounted for less than 40%. The figures are as follows: The bank's total issuance amount is 3,280,946.50 yuan. Reserves: 2,312,946.50 yuan in cash and 968,000 yuan in guarantees. Two Lawyers Practicing Law

▲ Pan Ying: Jurist Pan Ying, styled Bingfu, is a profound scholar of law. He has authored numerous legal papers, scattered across various issues of legal commentaries. His theories are widely circulated and praised. He once served in the Beijing press. Last year, the Shanghai Law College hired him as a department head, where he made many plans. After the January 28th Incident, when the college relocated to Hangzhou, Lawyer Pan resigned and continued his legal research. In the autumn, at the invitation of Lawyer Wang Shuchiao in Shanghai, he began a collaborative law practice, joining the Shanghai Bar Association as a member. He handles litigation and non-litigation cases in courts at all levels. His office is located at Quanli in the French Concession on Rue Remi. It is reported that Lawyer Pan upholds justice and serves society with the aim of protecting human rights, which has earned him the trust of his clients.

▲ Zhang Shewo: Lawyer Zhang Shewo, from Chuansha, Jiangsu, is of sincere character. He initially studied at Shanghai University, proficient in both Chinese and Western languages. While at the university, he wrote and translated articles and plays for Eastern Miscellany and Short Story Magazine. Before long, he became a special contributor to the Shen Bao and Xin Bao newspapers, as well as various magazines, writing no less than hundreds of thousands of words. He has been renowned in literary circles for years, and his words consistently reveal his sincere and honest attitude toward the world and things. Therefore, those who know Mr. Zhang all acknowledge him as a sincere gentleman. Mr. Zhang had aspired to the law from an early age and entered the Law School of Soochow University, studying diligently for several years. He has now graduated, earning a Bachelor of Laws degree, and has been licensed by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to practice law. He has established his office at No. 218 Jiangxi Road, 4th Floor, telephone number 13939, collaborating with Lawyer Wu Shou Gong and others. Lawyer Zhang has expressed his unwavering commitment to serving others with integrity and trustworthiness.

▲ Cai Tingkai Cigarettes: During the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the 19th Route Army bravely fought for two days, adding glory to the country. The tragic injuries and deaths deeply moved the Minzhong Tobacco Company, which, after comforting the troops at the front line, could not bear to witness the scene. Recognizing the enormous funds needed for the treatment of the wounded and the consolation of the dead, and believing that no Chinese person could stand idly by, they, with the consent of the 19th Route Army Headquarters, specially manufactured Jiang Guangnai, Cai Tingkai, and 19th Central Army brand cigarettes, donating ten yuan per case to comfort the national martyrs. Now that General Cai Tingkai's cigarettes have been launched, with their fragrant aroma, it is hoped that people from all walks of life will gladly purchase them.

In Shanghai, they will be delivered by special messenger, and in other cities, they will be sent by mail, while supplies last. Request them quickly.

▲ Domestic Rice Flour: Mazaki Road, Chung Cheng Yih Machinery Flour at the end of McIntyre Road, has been meticulously researched, so its products are very fine, and the prices are fair. It is reported that the factory's cake flour sells for 63 cents per 100 taels, and the bran flour sells for 32 cents per 100 taels, adhering to the principle of small profits and large sales. Therefore, the prices are cheaper than those of others, so the major printing factories in Shanghai are happy to use the factory's products. The factory is the pioneer of machine-made cake flour in Shanghai. Its products have been around for over ten years, and it has continued to research and improve them, sparing no expense, which cannot be compared to those who rashly imitate without seeking practicality.

To the Editor:

Yesterday, your newspaper published a report that our company's Yibin steamer had an accident downstream of Yichang. Our company has received a telegram from Yichang stating that this did not happen. The steamer is still operating between Yichang and Chongqing. The information in your newspaper must be a mistaken rumor. We request a correction.

Xujiahui Observatory Weather Forecast at 4:30 PM Yesterday: The Shandong coast will have clear and cold weather with northeasterly winds. The Yangtze River basin and the coastal area south of Ma'anshan will have clear weather with localized rain or fog. The wind will come from the northwest to northeast. A hurricane northeast of Mindanao will move northwestward. Its center was located within 60 miles of the intersection of 11 degrees north latitude and 127 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM. Wind force unknown. In the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 48.9 degrees, and the lowest was 46.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 61.3 degrees, and the lowest was 32.4 degrees.

Reader Advisory

㈠ Discussion of the question raised by Ms. Zhang Yunqiu

--See this column on December 3

Mr. Wang Nantang's message: Couples quarrel mostly because the cost of living increases and the income is not enough to cover household expenses. The only way to remedy this is to save money.

Mr. Wang Shaba's message: There are several reasons why a couple's love declines: 1. Environmental factors; 2. Extramarital affairs; 3. Minor disagreements; 4. The psychology of preferring the new to the old, with the first point being the most significant. The remedy for the first cause is to "accept fate and abide by one's position," while the remedy for the other three causes is to use the eight characters "respect each other, love each other, and remain the same from beginning to end."

Mr. Chen Zengping's message: The first reason is that their thinking is not sound, and they do not understand the true meaning of love. They only know how to enjoy the sweetness of love but have not thought about the obligations they should fulfill. Therefore, once they are together, they feel the burden of responsibility is too heavy. For the second, (A) one should be cautious from the beginning, and both parties must understand each other deeply; (B) recall the trivial matters of past love and use them as conversation material to arouse the revival of old feelings, and never use emotions to argue, resulting in a stalemate.

Mr. Li Xing's message: The first reason is that at the beginning of love, both parties hide their true nature and compromise to achieve their ultimate goal. After living together for a long time, each reveals their true face, and since everything is settled, there is no need to compromise. Thus, love cools, and the tragedy begins. The second remedy: (1) Be able to understand each other, so that "big things become small, and small things become nothing," the best policy; (2) Men and women each find a suitable job and put their spirits into their work to reduce conflict between families, a medium policy; (3) Often make short separations, the worst policy.

Mr. Liu Xinmin's message: The first reason is the psychology that "marriage is the tomb of love," and the inability of women to be economically independent is also a major reason. The second remedy: (1) Women must strive for economic independence; (2) In terms of family, men and women must share the burden together. Ms. Huang Liyuan's message: The first reason is that there was no long-term consideration at the beginning, and no attention was paid to the other party's academic qualifications and temperament. The second couple must respect and love each other in peacetime, and both treat each other with sincerity. The wife is good at managing household affairs, and the husband does not waste money outside. If there are differences of opinion, they should forgive each other.

㈡ Mr. Yang Xun's message: 21, 12, 4

I have a question that I have thought about for a long time but cannot resolve, and I ask you to provide an answer that is consistent with the facts. The question is:

"Suppose there are only two ways to do something: one is against conscience but beneficial; one is not against conscience but harmful; then which method should be implemented?"

I am afraid that you will not understand the meaning of this question, so I have cited a practical example below:

"Wang Lao Wu is the owner of a store that specializes in selling × goods. Since the September 18th Incident, he has felt that he would be ashamed to sell × goods again, but if he does not sell them, then the many stocks in the store will inevitably not be sold, and cash will certainly not be obtained. However, the end of the year is approaching, and the payment for ×× foreign firm's goods cannot be delayed! The shareholder's dividends must be paid as required, and there are also daily expenses……… So, what is the best thing to do, continue to sell? Or declare bankruptcy without selling?"

This question ends here, please also follow my method and give me a factual answer in the newspaper! Reply: The question raised in the letter is too general to answer. Now, I will only answer the factual matter cited below: Wang Lao Da sells × goods, which is indeed beneficial to himself, but only benefits the "individual," at most only benefiting the "family." However, on the other hand, it harms our entire country and the entire nation, because Wang Lao Wu's sale of × goods directly causes our country's economy to be hit, and indirectly allows the ×× people to turn the money earned from our country into guns and cannons to fight the volunteers in the Northeast. Is the interest of one person or family important? Or is the interest of one nation important? I think probably anyone can answer this question, not to mention that the fact here is that the benefit is in one family, but the harm is in one country?

The payment for the × well foreign firm's goods must be paid off. Shouldn't the blood debts of the Northeast be repaid? Wang Lao Wu's family's life needs to be paid for, and shouldn't the Northeast volunteers and the Northeast refugees have their living expenses? In the icy and snowy frontier, the Volunteer Army is struggling to defend the survival of our nation, while Wang Lao Wu sits safely at home selling × goods, opening up financial resources for the enemy, then he is really not as good as a deer or pig, so there is still talk of "conscience"?

If you do not understand the question of "is personal interest important"? Or "is national interest important?" is clearly understood, then what goods can only be sold? Aren't the likes of Puyi and Zheng Xiaoxu also called "people"?

Important Educational News

Ministry of Communications Plans to Expand the Wusong Merchant Marine School

Nanjing, 5th: The Ministry of Communications plans to expand the Wusong Merchant Marine School. In addition to the original navigation and engine departments, it will add mechanical and technical departments, each with advanced and junior classes.

Superintendent Zhou Fo-hai of the Jiangsu Education Department Inspects Northern Jiangsu (3)

Holds Public Lecture

Continues Inspecting Schools

(Special Correspondent from Nantong) Since arriving in Nantong, Zhou Fo-hai, Superintendent of the Jiangsu Education Department, has been inspecting education tirelessly, day and night. Today (the 3rd), he was jointly invited by all the major middle and elementary schools and the Education Bureau of the city to give a public lecture. At 8 a.m., Superintendent Zhou, along with his staff who came to Nantong, took time to visit the park. When they arrived at the Nantong Theater, the lecture venue, more than three thousand teachers, students, and educational administrators had already arrived, marking the first grand occasion of public gatherings in Nantong's history. First, Chairman Zhang, the County Magistrate, gave a solemn introductory speech. Then, Mr. Zhou took the stage, and the audience applauded, giving him a warm welcome. The main points of his speech were roughly divided into three sections. The first section briefly described the historical value of Nantong's developed education and industry, regretting its decline due to the impact of the world's economic trends. Therefore, he expressed hope that the revival of Nantong is the common responsibility of the people of Nantong, especially the educational sector, which bears an even greater responsibility. He also said that the revival of Nantong is the starting point for the Chinese nation to rise, hoping that the Nantong education sector would make special efforts. The second section briefly stated that today's China is plagued by three ills: chaos, poverty, and lack of knowledge. These three are mutually causal. Social instability leads to chaos, undeveloped industry leads to poverty, and educators abandoning their responsibilities leads to a lack of knowledge among the general populace. However, because of the lack of knowledge among the people, industry has failed to develop and society has failed to stabilize. The failure of education to fulfill its mission is the root cause of poverty and chaos. In the past, Nantong's industry was

developed, and society was stable, thanks to the great contribution of education. He deeply hoped that in the future, the spirit of creation and construction of the predecessors would be carried forward to revive Nantong, which is the way to save China. The third section briefly stated that the purpose of education is to save the country, and saving the country requires talent. Talent must possess the following three conditions: first, abundant knowledge; second, sound personality; and third, correct thinking. The mission of education itself is to impart knowledge, cultivate personality, and guide thinking. None can be lacking. The best way for students to save the country is only through studying and cultivating personality. It is necessary to promote our country's inherent virtues, and to know etiquette and abide by order. Young people should concentrate on the belief in the Three Principles of the People, and strive to study and be good people with the spirit of "Saving the country requires studying, and studying is saving the country," in order to save the country. Finally, he comforted the educational administrators and teachers, saying that in today's society where industry is declining, there must be "two people eating one person's food, and one person doing two people's work" for China to have a solution. The lecture lasted for two hours, and the audience listened attentively without fatigue, showing great unity. In the afternoon, he inspected various places. He first went to the county's sports field. It happened to be the ball game between Tongzhong and Chongjing schools. He watched for a while and then went to the County Women's Normal School. It was Saturday afternoon and classes were already over. Principal Luo of the school led him to inspect the school buildings and equipment, and the extracurricular activities of the female students. He then inspected the Memorial Elementary School set up by the school for a week. Then he went to the County Normal School (this school was the first normal school established in our country, having been established for more than 30 years, producing many outstanding talents) to inspect military training, calligraphy and other classes, and school buildings. As it was getting late, he hurried to the Agricultural Science Department of Nantong College to visit. The college gate was covered with slogans welcoming Superintendent Zhou. Li Yongxing, the head of the agricultural science department, Zhang Wenqian, the head of the textile department, and professors Wang Zhaocheng and Lin Bingzheng came out to greet him and led him to visit various laboratories, explaining in detail, and presented various publications. Then he went to inspect the middle school attached to the college. On both sides of the gate, a couplet was hung high, "Saving the country requires studying, and studying is saving the country," which was quite eye-catching. After the inspection, it was already dusk and there was a light rain, so he returned to his residence. That evening at eight o'clock, he gathered more than two hundred people from the elementary school circles in the city to give instructions, and they dispersed at ten o'clock. It is expected that tomorrow morning, he will start inspecting rural elementary schools and public education centers, and then visit Wolf Mountain and pay homage to Mr. Zhang Jian's tomb. (December 3rd)

Shandong Education Department Orders the Dissolution of High Schools

Repentant Students May Return to School Within Two Weeks After Screening

Jinan, 4th Telegram. High school classes have not yet resumed today. The Education Department has issued an order for dissolution. Students are to leave the school and return to their hometowns. After screening by the Education Department, except for the two classes that voluntarily requested withdrawal and received certificates of completion, which will not be allowed to resume studies, the other three classes that were expelled will be allowed to resume studies if they submit a letter of repentance, a petition for a joint examination, and a guarantee from their parents, after being screened by the school and deemed capable of being reformed. The other nine classes must also submit a letter of repentance and a guarantee from their parents, and will only be allowed to resume studies after being screened by the school.

It is expected that classes can resume within two weeks.

Jiangsu Provincial School Faculty and Staff Discuss Demanding Back Pay

Please Issue Overdue Education Funds of More Than Four Months Promptly

Expresses Opinions on Service and Treatment Measures for Faculty and Staff

The 11th Second Executive Committee Meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Faculty and Staff Association was held at 10 a.m. on the 4th in the high school division of Suzhou Middle School. Attendees included Wu Dezhang, Wu Ziwo (Zhenjiang Middle School), Xue Jianwu (Nanjing Middle School), Chen Yue (Shanghai Middle School), Zhang Gongsu (Suzhou Middle School), Wu Cangsu (Yangzhou Middle School), Zhang Yiyan (representing Dezhang). Observers included Hu Huanyong (Principal of Suzhou Middle School), Shen Tongqia (Chairman of the Suzhou Middle School Faculty and Staff Association). Zhang Gongsu served as chairman, and Xue Jianwu served as recorder. Formalities were followed. ㈠ The Executive Chairman reported on recent work. A. The issue of "Education and Training Integration" has been referred to the Standing Committee of the School Association for discussion. All "Education and Training Integration Research Associations" will not be convened. B. The Science Conference has been successfully completed at Shanghai Middle School, and the discussion was fruitful. C. The provincial education funds are tight, with more than four months of arrears. D. The Education Funds Committee will meet next month to discuss the appointment of the director in charge of amending the organization. Although it has been reviewed and cancelled, the individual involved will still strive for it. ㈡ Affairs Committee Member Mr. Wu Ziwo reported on the income and expenditure of funds. ㈢ Mr. Chen Zhenbai reported on the compilation and printing of the member directory. ㈣ Principal Hu of Suzhou Middle School reported on the following matters. A. Regarding the issue of "Education and Training Integration," the Standing Committee of the School Association has discussed a proposal to suggest to the Education Department (whether or not to establish a director of instruction will be determined by each school based on its circumstances). B. Regarding the issue of the treatment of full-time teachers, the committee will also draft standards and submit them to the Education Department for review and approval (80 to 160 yuan for junior high school, 120 to 200 yuan for senior high school). C. Regarding the issue of faculty and staff participation, the committee will also draft measures and suggest them to the Education Department (faculty and staff who have served for five years will be allowed to travel for observation once, while still receiving their original salary, and the Education Department will provide travel expenses). D. Regarding the issue of education funds, the Management Office has failed to earnestly fulfill its responsibilities and promises to the representative assembly of the School Association. ㈤ Matters for discussion. 1. The Faculty and Staff Association of Songjiang Middle School sent a letter stating that the school will still collect income tax. How should this be handled? It was resolved that A. In accordance with the resolutions of previous sessions of this association, since the treatment has not yet been improved, the payment will be postponed, and the association will be notified. B. If necessary, opinions may be expressed to the outside world in writing. 2. Education funds have been in arrears for more than four months. Personnel at the Education Funds Management Office are drawing salaries, but they are unaware that colleagues in provincial schools are going to work hungry, which is extremely difficult. What methods should be used to alleviate this urgent situation? It was resolved that A. A letter of severe warning should be sent to the Management Office. B. A temporary plenary meeting of representatives will be held at Nanjing Middle School on the 16th of this month to demand payment of the arrears from the Management Office. If all else fails, a petition will be submitted to the Third Plenary Session to reorganize the number of representatives of the Management Office. For those on the Nanjing-Shanghai Line, one person from each rural normal school below the 13th grade, at least two people from each school below the 13th grade, and at least three people from schools above the 13th grade. For schools in northern Jiangsu, at least three people from Yangzhou Middle School, at least two people from Tongzhou Middle School, and one person from each of the remaining schools. The following two resolutions will also be submitted by the association for their execution: A. Positive aspect: This demand for arrears

The conference must be adjourned only after the Management Office has completely disbursed the expenses for August, September, and October of this year. B. Negative aspect: If the above objectives cannot be achieved, all representatives will petition the Third Plenary Session to reorganize the Management Office and demand that the responsible personnel of the Management Office resign to make way for the capable. 3. The "Measures for Service and Treatment of Faculty and Staff in Secondary Schools" promulgated by the Ministry of Education are not in line with the actual situation. Should this association express its opinions? It was resolved that this association should submit the following opinions to the Ministry of Education and the Education Department separately, and the temporary plenary representatives should study them in general and strive for them with the Ministry of Education and the Education Department separately: A. Implement a full-time teacher system and do not calculate salary by the hour. B. Class hours: 14 to 18 hours per week for senior high school, 16 to 20 hours per week for junior high school. C. Salary: 140 to 220 yuan per month for senior high school, 100 to 160 yuan per month for junior high school. D. The actual budget should be calculated based on the median number of class hours and the median salary of full salary. E. Those who have their grade deducted or their position changed should have their teaching time reduced by six hours. 4. The member directory has been printed. What should be done with those who have not sent in their names? It was resolved that Mr. Chen Zhenbai should send a letter urging them to send them in quickly. 5. What should be done with those who have not yet paid their membership dues for this session? It was resolved that Mr. Wu Ziwo should send a letter urging them to pay them quickly. 6. What should be done with the cases assigned by the Science Conference? It was resolved that this association should submit it to the next session of the representative assembly for decision. 7. The "Education and Training Integration Research Association" has been discussed by the Standing Committee of the School Association. Should this association investigate and convene a meeting? It was resolved that this association should postpone convening a meeting, but should send another letter to the School Association for careful discussion. (6) Adjournment.

▲Letter to the Education Funds Management Office: Dear Sirs, Our association previously believed that the provincial education funds were in arrears excessively, and resolved at the 11th Representative Assembly to send a letter to your office, urging you to issue the education funds for July, August, and September of this year by October, and to issue them on a monthly basis thereafter, without delay. We trust this was registered. Now it is December, and the education funds for August have not yet been issued, causing various schools to be in dire straits and on the verge of starvation. If this situation continues, what will become of the future of education in Jiangsu Province? Your office is in charge of managing the education funds of Jiangsu Province, and it is difficult to shirk this responsibility. It is hereby resolved by the Executive Committee of our association to issue a severe warning to your office, urging you to understand your position clearly, quickly devise emergency measures, and make plans to fix the situation, so as to avoid accusations of holding a position without performing its duties. Otherwise, for the sake of the future of education in the province, our colleagues will do everything in their power to deal with this situation. Where responsibility lies, public opinion cannot be avoided. We hope that your office will truly seek benefits for the public. (Omitted below)

Educational Delegation Passing Through Paris, Cheng Qibao Expresses Opinions

China Should Adopt the Best Education Systems from Various Countries as Appropriate

The Investigation Team Will Go to Italy and Austria for Investigation

Havas News Agency, Paris, 4th Telegram. It was previously reported that the Chinese Educational Delegation had been inspecting educational institutions in Lyon. Mr. Cheng Qibao, the head of the delegation, passed through Paris and told the reporter that the delegation went to the Rhone region to investigate rural issues and rural education issues after visiting Lyon. There are five members in the delegation. Although they should make a report together after the investigation, each person has specialized research issues, namely: sociology, primary education, secondary education, higher education, and technical education. China pays special attention to rural issues, because most of the Chinese people are farmers. Chinese farmers cannot immediately adopt the methods used in Western agriculture. The only way to make progress is to seek it gradually. The delegation will go to Italy and Austria for investigation. Mr. Cheng believes that each country has its own special education methods. China does not want to copy those that are not suitable for the Chinese national character. Each country should have its own inherent education, but it is also possible to refer to and adopt the advantages of other countries to seek improvement. In recent years, China's education system has purely imitated the United States. Although there has been remarkable progress, China also wants to refer to the best systems of various European countries and adopt them as appropriate in order to achieve better results. The delegation's investigation has just begun, so Mr. Cheng cannot make a general critique of his observations, but only express his personal opinions on certain points. Mr. Cheng said that the Chinese people are diligent in their work, and are always happy, which is very similar to the French national character. Mr. Cheng said that he will go to England for investigation, and he will definitely find something very interesting there. At that time, recalling the visits to Lyon and Rhone, he will feel even more beneficial. When saying goodbye, Mr. Cheng agreed to meet again when he returns to France.

▲Will Meet with Zhang Xiaolin and Zhu Yan, the Two Chinese Directors, Together with the Education Bureau

▲Three Representatives Will Call on Mayor Wu Today

Elementary School Principals and Teachers Can Also Serve as Political Training for the Defense Corps

▲The County Government Ordered the Education Bureau to Comply Yesterday

The Shanghai County Government issued a special order to the Education Bureau yesterday, in accordance with the provisions of the "Implementation and Promotion Measures for Training of Defense Corps in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province," that elementary school principals and teachers can also serve as political training for the Defense Corps, and to issue training textbooks and training area troop roster, saying: For compliance, the case is to investigate the provisions of Article 14 of the "Implementation and Promotion Measures for Training of Defense Corps in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province," The political training of the Defense Corps in each township and town shall, in addition to being carried out by the instructors and trainers at any time, be undertaken by the county assigning the Education Bureau to entrust the principals and teachers of elementary schools near each training location, or equivalent personnel, etc. Now, the special training class of the Defense Corps of this county has completed its training period and is scheduled to start universal training in all districts on December 5. Regarding political training, in accordance with the regulations, the bureau should entrust the principals and teachers of elementary schools, or equivalent personnel, to handle it. A training textbook, "Common Knowledge of Nationals," and a troop roster for each training area are hereby issued to your bureau director for compliance, and the compliance shall be reported for verification without delay.

20th Anniversary of Guangzhao Public School

Guangzhao Public School held its 20th anniversary celebration yesterday morning at the Rongguang Grand Theater. More than 2,600 students, parents, and alumni attended the meeting. The meeting started at 9:30 a.m. After the ceremony, Principal (founder) Lu Songqian gave a speech, reporting on the school's 20-year history and future development plans. Next, Li Dachao, the representative of Mayor Wu, Guo Shun, the director of the school, Li Heyun, the representative of the parents of the students, and Zheng Jiaju, the representative of the alumni, gave speeches in succession. The celebration ended with the screening of a self-made film of the school and a Rongguang sound film. The speeches of Mayor Wu's representative and School Director Guo Shun are recorded below:

▲Speech by Li Dachao, Representative of Mayor Wu: Today is the 20th anniversary of the founding of Guangzhao Public School. I am very happy to be here on behalf of Mayor Wu to participate in this grand commemorative ceremony. Mayor Wu has always been very concerned about the events of Guangzhao Public School and is very willing to take responsibility together with his fellow villagers to expand this school to create a large-scale, fully equipped, and especially focused on the use of what is learned, to educate useful young people who can be producers and creators and be the most powerful and healthy backbone of today's society. Therefore, when he was the head of the Shanghai Municipal Government, he planned to promote this plan as a place for the education of young children of his fellow villagers, because he cares about education and always pays attention to the education of Guangzhao Public School. We have previously organized the Guangzhao Middle School Fundraising Committee, and Mayor Wu, in his busy schedule, served as the chairman to preside over the fundraising matters. I followed Mayor Wu and knew that he was most concerned about and worked hard for the expansion of Guangzhao Middle School, because he often told me that school education is the life of the country, and Guangzhao Middle School is the life of our Cantonese fellow villagers. In any case, we must strive to realize our ideal education in order to say that we have fulfilled a little responsibility. In this commemorative meeting, I don't have any good intentions to tell everyone, I'm very sorry. Also, Mayor Wu has a tracheal inflammation and cannot talk too much, so he asked me to participate as a representative. I hope that the villagers will forgive me.

▲Speech by School Director Guo Shun: Today I am very happy to participate in such a grand meeting. Among the commemorative meetings I have participated in, this is the first time that there have been so many people and it has been so lively. Looking back over the past 20 years, Guangzhao Public School has cultivated a lot of talents. However, the villagers' faith is very deep, and their expectations are very high. Guangzhao Public School plans to add a high school, which has been actively carried out by Mayor Wu and others, and there should be satisfactory results. Fifth Day of Family Education Lecture

The Great East Bookstore's family education lecture was the fifth day yesterday. It was given by Chen Heqin, the director of the Chinese Education Department of the Municipal Council, and the topic was "Experiments in Family Education." The main points were to tell us what should not be taught to children. There are several most important things: one, do not scare children; two, do not often scold children; three, do not hit children. Do not teach him like this. So how should we teach him? There are also several most important things: one, parents should set an example; two, teach him using a game-style method; three, children should move and do it themselves; four, teach children using a positive method; five, always encourage children. Regarding these issues, Mr. Chen gave examples during his speech, which were very thorough and worthy of being an expert in children's education research. It is heard that today's lecture is given by Dong Renjian, a professor at Daxia University, on "How Should Family Education Be Implemented?" This topic is very important for children's education, and there will definitely be more listeners.
